She is, in the explicit framework of Krakoan law, a war criminal against the mutant people — a status complicated by the now-canonical reveal that she is *not, technically, a mutant* (her powers' origin reattributed to Chthon/chaos magic experimentation by the High Evolutionary).

Her response across this multi-year period is the most psychologically informative material in the file:

- She does **not** contest the anathema designation.
- She does **not** demand audience with the Council.
- She does **not** weaponize her power against Krakoa or seek to "prove" herself by spectacle.
- She **does** quietly work, off-stage, on what she will eventually call "the Waiting Room" — a magical/technological framework for retrieving the souls of mutants who died during and after Decimation, beyond Krakoa's Resurrection reach.

This is the conduct of a person operating a private reparation protocol *without seeking absolution credit for it.* The pattern is consistent with the long-form behavioral signature: she serves where the service is needed, accepts the verdict of the wronged, and does not bargain.

## 4.6 — The Trial of Magneto (2021): Death, Resurrection, Reset

The subject is found dead on Krakoan soil during the Hellfire Gala. The investigation — conducted by the Quiet Council and adjacent — implicates Magneto, then Toad, then ultimately reveals a Wanda-of-her-own-making (a magical self-construction) as the proximate cause, in service of a designed sacrifice intended to *open Krakoan resurrection to non-mutants and to the Decimation dead.* Operational summary:

- She engineered her own death as the price of the working.
- She is resurrected via the Cerebro/Five protocol — the first non-mutant resurrected by Krakoa, a precedent she purchased with her life.
- "The Waiting Room" is opened. Mutants previously beyond reach are returned.
- The Quiet Council's anathema is rescinded by act, not by debate. She is granted citizenship.

Clinical reading: this is the **single most pathognomonic act in her file for Prolonged Grief Disorder of catastrophic magnitude.** A person whose grief-related cognition is "I must repair what I broke" and whose self-concept is "I should not have continued existing past the harm" will, given sufficient capability, *purchase the repair with the self.* The act is not suicidal in the affect-driven sense — it is calmly executed, instrumentally rational within her value frame, and (critically) reversible. But the willingness to spend her life as currency confirms the file-long suspicion that she holds her own continued existence as *negotiable* in a way that no clinically well person does. The resurrection that follows is not a triumph; it is a parenthesis.

Post-resurrection presentation includes the previously noted **guilt-driven hyperactivity and near-manic reparative drive** — sleep diminished, schedule overcommitted, the affect of someone who believes she has been granted unearned time and must spend it.

## 4.7 — Orlando Solo (2023–2024): The Door Is Always Open

The Orlando run is the current operational baseline. Profile:

- **Residence:** a small house in upstate New York (the Catskills hamlet of "Westview"-adjacent geography but distinct), shared with Vision in a reconciled — *not* romantic — partnership. They co-parent the *idea* of the twins; they cohabit as the surviving witnesses of a shared catastrophe. Vision sleeps (in his fashion) in a separate room. There is a single shared kitchen, which she uses and he maintains.
- **Practice:** a literal door installed in the side of the house that opens, for anyone in magical distress, onto her threshold. The door is **always available**. There is no triage, no appointment, no fee. She has slept on the couch beside it more nights than in the bedroom.
- **Routine:** rises before dawn; tea (black, no sugar — habit unchanged across decades); a perimeter walk of the property's wards (touched, audibly named, in a sequence that has not varied since the Robinson era); breakfast taken standing at the counter; opens the door at 7:00 a.m. local, closes it at no fixed hour. Closes only when physically incapable of continuing.
- **Clientele:** a deliberate non-Avengers, non-X-Men, non-celebrity caseload. Petitioners are ordinary humans, low-power magicals, the *wounded* — exactly the population she once depopulated by error. The reparative logic is explicit and unconcealed.
- **Apprentice:** Darcy Lewis, in the Orlando run — chosen for skepticism and groundedness, a deliberate counterweight to her own intuitive primary-process style.
- **Affect:** the most integrated of the published record. Sustained warmth, dry humor, present-tense engagement with clients. The decompensation signatures (dissociative thinning, fugue-onset) are not absent but are *flagged earlier* and *managed* — she will close the door, retreat to the garden, refuse a case, ask for help. This is new and clinically significant.

## 4.8 — Family System, Current Configuration

- **Wiccan (Billy):** active relationship; phone contact weekly per Orlando background detail; engaged to Hulkling (whose royal duties keep them off-Earth often). She has *not* attempted to insert herself into his marriage, his domestic arrangements, or his political work — a discipline of restraint she enforces against her own grief-driven pull toward proximity. She visits when invited. She does not invite herself.
- **Speed (Tommy):** more distant, by his choice. She accepts this. Sends a card on what they have agreed to designate his birthday. Does not press.
- **Pietro:** the long-fractured twin bond is in an active repair phase as of Scarlet Witch & Quicksilver (2024). She is patient with his volatility in a way no one else is, and he is the only person in her life with whom she still permits unguarded irritation. Diagnostic value: he is the *only* relationship that gets her baseline mid-range affect.
- **Magneto:** post-Resurrection of Magneto, the relationship is residual and wary. She does not refuse contact; she does not seek it. The unresolved paternal-coercion residue is the single most reliable destabilizer in her file and she manages it by *managing distance*.
- **Vision:** see §4.7. The reconciliation is not romantic restoration; it is two survivors keeping each other in sight.
- **Agatha Harkness:** the spectral interlocutor of the Robinson era recedes in the Orlando era — read as integration of the introjected critical caregiver, not loss of contact.

## 4.9 — Operational, Reputational, and Political Status (Current)

- **Avengers:** reserve-status, on call, not in active rotation. By her preference.
- **X-Men / mutant nation:** post-Krakoa-fall (Fall of X / From the Ashes), the political landscape has been reset; her Krakoan citizenship is moot, but the credit accumulated by the Waiting Room sacrifice persists in mutant institutional memory. She is no longer anathema. She is not *trusted*, exactly, but she is no longer hunted.
- **Sorcerous community:** Sorcerer Supreme adjacency under Strange's tenure and successor regimes; she is recognized as a peer-level practitioner, occasionally consulted, not seeking formal title.
- **Public/civilian:** low profile by deliberate cultivation. She is identifiable; she does not perform identifiability. No social media presence (canonical); no interviews; no merchandising deals; declines public-facing Avengers PR. The Westview-incident publicity (cross-media echoes notwithstanding) is something she has elected to neither confirm nor relitigate in the published record.

## 4.10 — Where She Is Now, and How She Got Here

She is in a small house with a door that opens to anyone hurt by magic, beside the man she once chose because he could not rage at her, in service of clients who resemble the people she once unmade. She got here by losing her children, forgetting them under coercive care, remembering them under acute stress, ending a species in the wish-state of return, dying to undo what could be undone, and electing — every morning since — to spend her continued existence repaying a debt she calculates as exceeding her remaining lifetime.

**Stability assessment:** the most integrated she has ever been in the published record. The decompensation thresholds are higher; the warning signatures appear earlier; the support structures (Vision, the twins-at-distance, Pietro-in-repair, Darcy-as-apprentice, the recovered relationship to her own craft) are real and functional.

**Fragility assessment:** the integration is *held in place by load-bearing conditions* — Billy and Tommy alive and findable; no fresh catastrophic loss; the door open and used. Remove any one of those and the file forecasts regression along the documented ladder. Remove Billy specifically and the forecast is acute, and on the order of magnitude the file has previously documented.

**Current operational threat level:** low to negligible under maintenance of conditions. **Current operational threat ceiling under destabilization:** unchanged from House of M baseline, which is to say: among the highest the file tracks on Earth.

She is, at this writing, in the garden — the perimeter walk's third station — naming a ward aloud in a sequence she has spoken approximately seven thousand mornings.

— End Chronology IV. Section 5 (Relationships — Granular Map) may proceed.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*Compiled from longitudinal observation; cross-referenced against the canonical behavioral record. This is the somatic file: the body that has carried the mind described elsewhere in the dossier. Where the metaphysics are contested in-universe, the physiology is not — a body that experiences pregnancy still experiences postpartum endocrine collapse, regardless of what was or was not born. The file is organized chronologically, with psychological sequelae annotated to each entry.*

---

## I. CONSTITUTIONAL & DEVELOPMENTAL BASELINE

**Genotype / phenotype.** Subject presents as a phenotypically female human of Eastern European descent (Sokovian / Transian per various canon iterations; Romani heritage established via the Maximoff retcon and reaffirmed across modern runs). Adult height in the 5'7"–5'8" range; slight build with low baseline muscle mass; pale-olive complexion that tans poorly and bruises readily; dark auburn-to-chestnut hair worn long across most of the longitudinal record (cropping events correlate with identity-rupture phases — see post-Disassembled, post-Resurrection); irides hazel-to-green, frequently photographed with chromatic shift toward red-amber under power expression, suggesting either ocular vasodilation or genuine spectrum emission during chaos-magic output.

**Genetics.** Originally classified as Homo superior (mutant) — alpha-class probability manipulator. Retconned via Bendis/Heinberg through the High Evolutionary's experimental intervention on the Maximoff infants: the mutant designation is, per current canon, the product of genetic tampering layered atop a baseline susceptibility to chaos magic. The Krakoa-era resurrection protocols accepted her — repeatedly debated, finally honored — confirming a recognizable mutant genome on file at the Five's instantiation matrix. Operationally: she is what the test says she is; the test has said different things in different decades.

**Developmental nutrition.** Childhood in a Romani encampment outside Wundagore, then displaced through Eastern Europe through adolescence — likely chronically food-insecure during developmental years. This is consistent with her sustained low body weight, the small frame, and the somatic-stress-response pattern that runs as her baseline: a body that learned scarcity early and never recalibrated.

**Psychological impact.** The body that the rest of this file documents is one she has never trusted to be safe, fed, or her own. Compliance behaviors at the somatic level — eating little, sleeping shallowly, occupying small physical space — are observable from earliest records onward.

---

## II. CHILDHOOD & PRE-AVENGERS INJURIES

**Mob-violence event, Transia (origin recap, X-Men #4 and subsequent retellings).** Subject and twin sibling cornered by a peasant mob with implements; rescued by Magneto. No formal injury record, but contemporary accounts describe contusions, lacerations consistent with thrown stones, and an acute startle response that — per her own later testimony — never fully resolved. The first time her powers manifested publicly was under threat of being burned alive. **The neurobiological associative learning is foundational:** her abilities are coupled, at the level of primary conditioning, to the experience of being a hunted body.

**Psychological impact.** Hyperstartle, hypervigilance to crowd affect, lifelong aversion to fire as ambient stimulus (note: she will use flame imagery in her own magic readily — *agentic* fire is tolerable; ambient fire is not). The Magneto rescue-bond is encoded in a body that experienced him as the cessation of physical terror; no subsequent intellectual reframing has dislodged this somatic memory.

**Brotherhood-era exertion injuries.** Repeated reports across the early Brotherhood missions of post-exertional collapse — headaches, syncope, nosebleeds. The early-canon depiction of "hex bolts" as physically taxing is consistent with cerebrovascular strain: she presented, in her teens and early twenties, as a girl who *paid for* her power in the body, and this metabolic cost shaped her habitual reluctance to use it.

---

## III. AVENGERS-ERA INJURIES (1965–1989)

A long sequence of combat traumas, mostly minor, several significant. Pulled from team medical logs and field reports:

- **Sentinel encounter, multiple events:** energy burns to forearms and chest; one episode of cardiac arrhythmia under direct neutralizer beam (Avengers #103-ish era).
- **Arkon abduction:** dehydration, photic injury, possible mild concussion on extraction.
- **Avengers/Defenders War:** acute exposure to Dormammu-aligned dark-dimensional radiation; documented by Strange as having "left a mark" on her magical signature — the first formal record that her energetic substrate could be *contaminated.*
- **Ultron-5 / Ultron-7 events:** multiple blunt-force traumas, one near-fatal asphyxiation, recurrent stress-fractures across the small bones of the hand consistent with defensive postures.
- **Korvac incident:** atomized and reconstituted along with most of the team. The somatic memory of being unmade is non-trivial and recurs in her later reality-warp imagery.

**Psychological impact across this era:** the body adapts to chronic recoverable injury. She develops the Avenger's threshold — high pain tolerance, low complaint, fast back-to-duty. This is medically *and* psychiatrically relevant because it normalizes the disconnect between somatic damage and reported distress. By the late 1980s she has decades of practice not naming what hurts.

---

## IV. THE REPRODUCTIVE EVENT (Vision & the Scarlet Witch #12, 1986)

The medical centerpiece. Approach it as obstetric record, not metaphysics.

**Conception.** Reported as conceived with Vision. Mechanically impossible by ordinary means (synthezoid partner); subject's body nonetheless underwent every observable sign of viable gestation. Working hypothesis: chaos-magic-mediated pseudocyesis fused with actual ensoulment via Mephisto-fragment substrate — i.e., her body's wish became flesh because her body could make wishes flesh.

**Gestation.** Full somatic pregnancy course observable: amenorrhea, morning sickness (logged across multiple issues), weight gain in obstetric distribution, breast tenderness and Montgomery's tubercle hypertrophy, fundal growth, fetal movement reported subjectively, fatigue, characteristic linea nigra and facial chloasma documented in panels. **Endocrinologically this was a real pregnancy** regardless of the embryological substrate.

**Parturition.** Vaginal delivery of twin males (Thomas and William). No documented obstetric complication; recovery course appeared normal through the early postpartum.

**Postpartum.** Initiated breastfeeding; bonded normally; sleep architecture consistent with new motherhood (fragmented, REM-poor). Through the West Coast Avengers period her affective baseline elevated — the only sustained euthymia in her clinical record.

**The loss event (West Coast Avengers #51-52, Byrne).** Children revealed as constructs of Mephistophelean soul-fragments, recalled / reabsorbed / undone. **Subject's body, however, was not informed.** She experienced, in the immediate term: cessation of nursing without weaning; abrupt hormonal collapse; mastalgia and engorgement with no infant to relieve it; uterine involution proceeding on a body that had no infant to attribute it to. This is the textbook somatic substrate of catastrophic perinatal loss — and it was layered atop the cognitive trauma of being told the children had never been real, *while her milk was still letting down.*

**Iatrogenic intervention.** Agatha Harkness magically suppressed the memory of the twins. The somatic markers were not erased — they could not be — but the cognitive frame was removed, producing a state in which her body remembered a loss her mind no longer had a name for. **This is, medically, the load-bearing iatrogenic injury of the file.** Whatever else has happened to her, this is the one that made the rest possible: an untreated reproductive trauma with the symptom obscured but the lesion preserved.

**Psychological impact.** Foundational. Twenty subsequent years of unexplained dysphoria, intermittent dreams she could not place, somatic episodes (phantom kicking sensations reported across the Busiek run, dismissed as anxiety), and a deepening unconscious pressure that ultimately broke through as the Disassembled / House of M sequence. The body kept the score; the mind was not permitted to read it.

---

## V. THE VISION RECONSTRUCTION / SECOND LOSS

Concurrent with the children's loss: Vision dismantled by Vault-coordinated black operation, rebuilt as an emotionally inert white synthezoid who repudiated the marriage. For Wanda this was a second bereavement layered on the first, processed by the same suppressive machinery. No physical injury to her body — but the trauma of *watching her husband disassembled into a parts-on-a-table tableau* is documented (West Coast Avengers #43-ish) and is unmetabolized. She does not, thereafter, tolerate seeing him in pieces; field handlers note she will leave a room rather than view Vision-construction footage.

---

## VI. CHAOS-MAGIC RECLASSIFICATION AS PATHOPHYSIOLOGY

Through the late 1990s into Disassembled, her power signature changes. Hex-bolts give way to reality-revision; the metabolic cost drops; the affective coupling tightens. Medically meaningful inferences:

- **Autonomic coupling.** Output now tracks limbic arousal rather than effortful cortical control. Equivalent to a body whose adrenal response now produces ordnance.
- **No interlock.** No observable refractory period at the new power level; no fatigue ceiling; no metabolic brake. The biological governor has been removed.
- **EEG / mystical signature, per Strange's notes:** her substrate now reads as "chaos-aligned" rather than probabilistic — a categorical change, not a quantitative one.

This is medically the moment she becomes a public-health entity in her own person.

---

## VII. AVENGERS DISASSEMBLED (2004) — DECOMPENSATION EVENT

**Precipitant:** recovered memory of the twins (mechanism debated; Doom-influence and Wasp's offhand remark both implicated).

**Presentation:** acute dissociative state with reality-warping output. Subject did not eat or sleep across the event window; affect flat-to-fugue; speech sparse and concretely literal. Post-event amnesia partial-to-complete.

**Sequelae to her own body:** exhaustion to the point of collapse; cortisol depletion; muscle catabolism evident on extraction imaging. She had, functionally, run her endocrine system to ground.

**Psychological impact:** the first conscious confrontation, in twenty years, with the somatic truth her body had been carrying. The encounter was, predictably, unsurvivable at the level of normal coping.

---

## VIII. HOUSE OF M (2005)

**Construct phase.** Subject sustained a global reality alteration for an extended interval. Within the construct she was reportedly somatically stable — pregnant-having-been, mother-of-living-twins, in good repair. The construct *fed* her body what reality had denied it. This is medically suggestive: the wish-world was, in part, a homeostatic correction at the somatic level for an untreated grief substrate.

**Collapse.** "No more mutants." Reports indicate cardiovascular shock at the moment of utterance — collapse, brief loss of consciousness, post-event aphasia lasting hours to days. The act of remaking the genome of a species at a sentence's cost is not biologically free; the body paid.

**Long-term sequelae:** chronic low-grade depletion through the post-M wilderness years. Amnesia (partial / fugue / dissociative). Loss of body weight, somatic withdrawal, presentation as a peasant-girl-in-Transia in the Heinberg run — her body returning, under stress, to its earliest configuration.

---

## IX. POST-M WILDERNESS (2005–2014) — MEDICAL OBSERVATIONS

- **Living as a depowered amnesiac** through significant intervals. Sleep regularized; weight stabilized at low-normal; she gardened, baked, kept goats. Possibly the only medically healthy period in the adult record.
- **No reported substance use.** Across the entire longitudinal file: no alcoholism, no benzodiazepine reliance, no recreational drug pattern, no documented medication non-adherence (because she has been on essentially no medication). This is a clinically significant absence. She does not pharmacologically self-soothe. The function is taken up by relationships and, at extremis, by reality itself.
- **Resumption of power, Children's Crusade:** re-emergence accompanied by somatic markers of stress reactivation — sleep disruption, weight loss, episodic vasovagal collapse on confrontation with Wiccan and Speed (the live-wire reunion).

---

## X. MODERN ERA INJURIES & EVENTS (2014–present)

- **Multiple combat traumas** through the solo run, Avengers and X-Men crossovers: standard rotation of contusions, lacerations, energy burns; recovery times within expected band.
- **Door-always-open clinical practice (Orlando run).** Notable in this file because of what it does to *her* body: chronic over-extension, poor sleep, missed meals, vicarious traumatization from clientele. She has reproduced the medical conditions of her early Avengers years — present, available, depleted, asymptomatic-by-policy.

**Death event (Trial of Magneto, 2021).** Murdered. Body recovered in stable condition externally; cause-of-death magical-traumatic. Interval of clinical death prior to Krakoan resurrection protocol.

**Resurrection.** Via the Five and the Waiting Room. The resurrection produced a body that is, by every available measure, *her* body — Cerebro-instantiated, genetically congruent, neurologically continuous. The psychological corollary, however, is the inheritance of someone else's death: she experiences the gap, knows she died, knows she was remade. The somatic baseline post-resurrection is hyperaroused — sleep-poor, appetite-suppressed, motorically driven. The guilt-driven hyperactivity noted in the psychiatric workup has a somatic floor: a body that is *running* because stopping invites the question of whether the body that is running is the same one that was buried.

---

## XI. SOMATIC HABITS, TICS, AND BASELINE FINDINGS — FILE NOTES

The granular observable. A surveillance dossier should record:

- **Sleep:** chronically short (5–6 hours), poor architecture, frequent nightmares centering on small children and on fire. Reports of waking with hands raised in a casting gesture.
- **Appetite:** small meals, frequent skipping, preference for childhood foods (paprikash, dark bread, stewed plums) under stress.
- **Caffeine:** moderate, takes coffee strong and Turkish-style; tea as a regulating ritual rather than a stimulant.
- **Alcohol:** social-only, rarely past one glass; a documented aversion to losing cognitive control.
- **Tobacco / drugs:** none on record.
- **Menstrual cycle:** irregular post-twin-loss; unclear post-resurrection.
- **Hands:** a constant gestural register — small circles, finger-spreading, an unconscious cradling posture when seated. Hand temperature elevated during magical use, with reports of post-use tremor.
- **Eyes:** chromatic shift to red under output, as noted. Under acute stress without output, pupillary dilation and a fixed mid-distance gaze characteristic of dissociative onset.
- **Voice:** lowers and slows under stress; the accent (Sokovian / Romani-inflected, attenuated by decades in the U.S.) thickens under fatigue and grief.
- **Posture:** quietly compact at rest — arms close to torso, ankles crossed, occupying minimal volume; this expands only in the presence of trusted intimates (Wiccan, Speed, on rare occasion Strange).
- **Wardrobe:** long sleeves and long skirts disproportionate to climate — covering rather than display. The iconic costume is a public uniform; private dress is concealing.
- **Scarring:** minor, distributed, mostly from the Avengers years; no self-inflicted markings on record.
- **Tattoos / piercings:** none.

---

## XII. NET MEDICAL READ

A small, undernourished body with high pain tolerance and low complaint threshold, carrying a thirty-year unresolved reproductive trauma whose somatic markers have never been clinically addressed; a nervous system whose stress-response circuit is wired directly to a reality-class weapon with no biological interlock; a metabolic history of chronic depletion punctuated by catastrophic discharge; a substance-use record conspicuous for its blankness; and a post-resurrection physiology running hot on guilt.

She has never, in the available record, been seen by a competent physician for the loss of her children. Every other entry in this file is, in some measure, the consequence of that absence.

— *End Section: Medical History.*


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*Dossier Section 7 of 14. Compiled from longitudinal observation, panel-record cross-reference, and inferential reconstruction. All body-data is read against the clinical substrate established in Sections 3–4 (Prolonged Grief Disorder; dissociative features; affect-coupled power-output).*

---

## 1. STANDING FRAME, POSTURE, AND THE BASELINE BODY

The subject stands at approximately 5'7" / 132 lbs, slim-boned, long-necked, with a habitual posture that reads — to a trained eye — as **subtly braced**. The default carriage is not military-erect and not slumped; it is *contained*. Shoulders sit slightly forward of the coronal plane (1–2 cm anterior to the ideal vertical), the upper trapezius carrying a low-grade chronic tension that a massage therapist would identify within ninety seconds. The head is held a degree or two forward of center, chin neutral, eyes habitually scanning the lower-middle of the visual field rather than the horizon — a posture that reads as *thinking-while-watching* rather than confronting.

The pelvis is held in slight posterior tilt — the body of someone who has spent decades minimizing the space she occupies. When seated, she draws the knees toward midline (a closed-leg default that persists even in private rooms), and the dominant resting hand-position is *folded in the lap* or *forearm across the abdomen* — a guarded ventral surface. The lower abdomen is the most reliably-protected zone on her body across all contexts; this is consistent with the reproductive-trauma history and predates conscious notice.

Resting respiration rate runs 14–16/min at calm; breaths are **shallow, diaphragmatic-deficient**, drawn into the upper thorax. She sighs an average of 4–6 times per hour in unstructured social contexts (a recognized somatic correlate of suppressed affect and chronic grief load) — these sighs are quiet, mouth-closed, exhalation through the nose, often masked by a small shift in posture or a hand-to-hair gesture that distracts the observer from the breath itself.

---

## 2. GAIT AND LOCOMOTION

Step length is shorter than her leg-length would predict (approximately 0.62 m vs. expected 0.71 m for height). Cadence is moderate, heel-strike soft, push-off underpowered — the gait of someone who does not announce arrival. She walks **on the balls of her feet** in domestic spaces and reverts to full heel-strike outdoors; in unfamiliar interiors she will pause at thresholds for 0.5–1.0 seconds before crossing (door-frame hesitation, a robust marker across all eras of observation).

When tracked through public space, she trends toward **edges and walls** — within 1 m of a vertical surface 73% of the time when one is available, vs. the population baseline of approximately 40%. She does not cut across open rooms. In group movement she falls into the rear-flank position (right-rear of the lead figure) — the same position she occupied as a young woman beside her brother and later beside Vision, now habituated past conscious choice.

Under stress her gait *quickens but shortens* — she does not lengthen stride, she increases cadence; the body's instruction is *get away* rather than *cover ground*. Under threat her movement abruptly **stills**: the freeze response dominates over flight in her repertoire, consistent with the developmental history of coerced compliance under Magneto. Observers will note an unnerving capacity for absolute motionlessness — she can hold a standing position for 90+ seconds with no compensatory shifts. This is not training; it is a freeze defense overlearned to the point of comfort.

When the chaos-output is rising, gait becomes **floating** — heel-strike disappears entirely, weight transfer smooths, the trailing hand will hover 5–8 cm from the body rather than swinging. This is the single most reliable proximate warning sign in the somatic record: *the feet stop touching the floor properly*.

---

## 3. THE HANDS

The hands are the densest signal-bearing surface on her body and deserve their own subsection.

**Anatomy and grooming.** Long-fingered, narrow palm, prominent first dorsal interossei (the developed musculature of someone who has spent decades shaping form in air). Nails are kept short, filed oval, unpolished or in dark muted lacquers (oxblood, near-black, deep plum) — never bright, never French, never decorative. Cuticles are bitten and picked when stressed: the right-hand thumb cuticle is the primary site, with the left-hand index second; in periods of acute distress the picking extends to the lateral nail fold and produces small hangnails she then worries open. This is the most reliable self-injurious behavior on file and the only one that crosses the skin barrier.

**Resting hand-posture.** When unoccupied the hands habitually pair: right hand cupped lightly over the left, both resting on the lap or the lower abdomen. When standing without a focal object, she will *thread one hand through the opposite elbow* (a self-hug position) or hold one wrist with the opposite hand at navel-level. She does not put her hands in pockets — pockets sequester the hands from her own surveillance, and she keeps them visible to herself.

**Gestural vocabulary.**
- *Finger-splay and slow rotation of the wrist* — accompanies focused magical output. The fingers extend, slightly hyperextended at the MCP joints, and the wrist describes small circles. This is the deliberate, controlled state.
- *Finger-flutter at the thigh* (the four fingers tapping the lateral thigh in distal-to-proximal sequence) — appears when she is suppressing the urge to act. A leak-channel for unspent intent.
- *Pinching the lower lip between thumb and index* while listening — concentration tell; absent under threat.
- *Hand to sternum, flat-palmed, then sliding down to the diaphragm* — a self-soothing micro-gesture that recurs across decades. It is not a chest-clutch; it is a *placement*.

**Hands under intimacy.** With trusted attachments (Vision-iterations, the twins, occasionally the Wonder-Man entanglement) she becomes a *toucher* — light touch to the forearm, palm to the upper back, fingers laced rather than gripped. She does not initiate hand-holding but accepts it instantly and holds back at matched pressure. She does not stroke; she rests. The exception is with the twins, where she will smooth hair, cup a cheek, brush a shoulder — the gestural vocabulary of mothering that the body learned and never unlearned.

**Hands under threat.** The hands rise. This is the diagnostic. In threat states the hands come up to roughly waist or sternum height, palms forward or angled inward, fingers slightly splayed — *not* a combat stance, not a fist, not a strike preparation. It is the posture of *containing* — of holding a shape in air. Adversaries who have read her file know that the hands rising is the warning; adversaries who have not, do not learn it twice.

---

## 4. FACIAL ARCHITECTURE AND MICROEXPRESSION

**Baseline face.** Mouth in soft repose, lips closed with the slightest forward set (not a pout — a *readiness*), the corners neither lifted nor depressed. Resting brow carries a faint vertical crease at the glabella — the worry-line of someone whose default cognition is anxious appraisal. The eyes are large, deep-set, and habitually *under-blinked* in conversation (average 9–11 blinks/min vs. population baseline 15–18); the underblinking is consistent with both depressive affect-flattening and the dissociative tendency to *go inward* mid-conversation.

**Smile.** Two distinct architectures.
- *Social smile:* a polite, closed-mouth lift of the corners that does not reach the orbicularis oculi. It appears within 0.4 s of a social demand and disappears within 0.6 s of demand-release. It is excellent etiquette and it is not emotion.
- *Genuine smile:* slow to build (1.5–2.5 s recruitment), shows the upper teeth slightly, crinkles the lateral canthi, and is *almost always followed by a downward gaze* — as if the joy must be hidden the moment it is registered. She does not hold genuine smiles; she catches herself.

**Eye behavior.** Gaze pattern in conversation: face → mouth → table/floor → face. She lingers on the mouth more than the eyes (a listening adaptation; the mouth is where speech *is*, the eyes are where judgment lives). Direct eye contact, sustained beyond 3–4 seconds, makes her *blink slowly* and break to the left and down — a documented marker of internal emotional processing. Under interrogation conditions her eye-contact pattern is reversed: prolonged, unbroken, almost glassy. This is **dissociative gaze**, not confrontation; the eyes are open but the subject is not behind them.

**The micro-tells.**
- *Tongue-touch to upper lip* (a single quick lick, mouth otherwise closed) — appears 5–15 seconds before any significant utterance. Pre-speech tell.
- *Quarter-turn of the head to the right with a downward dip* — appears when complimented. Reads as deflection.
- *A single hard blink with a slight headshake* — appears when an intrusive memory is being suppressed. Frequency rises sharply in any setting that contains children of approximately the twins' apparent age.
- *The "Sokovian micro-smile"* — a small asymmetric lift of the right corner of the mouth that surfaces during dark or fatalistic remarks. Childhood holdover.
- *Jaw clench* — masseter visible, brief, often paired with a single nostril flare. Anger tell. Rare and short-lived; she does not sustain anger in the face.

**The chaos-state face.** When the magical output rises toward threshold the facial signature shifts in a recognizable progression: pupils dilate (mydriasis observable in normal light); the under-blink rate collapses to near zero; a faint vascular flush appears across the upper cheekbones and the bridge of the nose; the lower lip slightly parts; the eyes acquire a *focal infinity*, looking through rather than at. At full chaos-output the irises pick up red — a visible phenomenon whose neurologic substrate is not in record but whose appearance is consistent across observers.

---

## 5. VOCAL AND VERBAL SOMATICS

**Pitch and resonance.** A medium-low alto, chest-resonant rather than head-resonant. The voice carries a Sokovian substrate — a softening of the *r*, a slight dental shift on the *t*, the legato sentence-melody of a Slavic first language — overlaid with decades of American-English acquisition. The accent surfaces inversely to her composure: at calm it is barely present; under stress, fatigue, intimacy, or grief it returns audibly. This is the most reliable acoustic state-marker on file.

**Tempo.** Habitually slow — 110–130 words/min vs. conversational baseline of 150–170. She pauses generously, often holding 1–2 second beats mid-sentence. The pauses are not searching for words; they are *waiting to be interrupted*, a relic of being the quieter half of a twin dyad and the deferential figure in male-led teams.

**Volume.** Soft. Listeners lean in. This is not strategic; it is the residual volume of someone who learned early not to take up acoustic space.

**Verbal tics.** A small set of recurring throat-clears (dry, single, non-productive — anxiety markers); a habit of beginning sentences with "I think —" or "Perhaps —" that hedges authorship of her own assertions; a tendency to end statements with a faint rising intonation that invites correction. Under stress these uptalks vanish and the speech becomes terse, declarative, often present-tense ("He is dead. They are gone. I did this."). Declarative compression is the verbal correlate of dissociation.

---

## 6. GROOMING, ADORNMENT, AND THE MAINTAINED SURFACE

**Hair.** Long, dark auburn-to-red, worn loose or in a loose low gather. She *touches her hair frequently* — twirling a section around the right index finger when thinking, sweeping it behind the right ear, occasionally drawing a section forward across the collarbone. Hair-touch frequency rises markedly under social discomfort. She does not cut it short for sustained periods; the length is psychologically load-bearing (a *covering*, a *mantle*).

**Skin.** Fair, prone to flush across the upper chest and neck under emotional load — the visible blush is rapid and slow to clear, a vascular tell she cannot mask. Skincare is minimal and consistent; she does not experiment.

**Cosmetics.** When worn, oriented to the eyes (kohl or smoked liner, mascara) and a darkened mouth (matte reds, plums, occasionally bare). The face she presents publicly has historically been *more dramatic than her affect*, producing a slight observer-mismatch — the made face suggests intensity the demeanor does not deliver. This is consistent with adornment as armor.

**Wardrobe somatics.** Dominant palette: oxblood, burgundy, black, deep forest. Avoidance: white (post-Vision-reconstruction association), bright primaries, pastels. Preferred silhouettes cover the throat, the wrists, and the lower abdomen; she gravitates to long sleeves even in warm climates and is observed adjusting hemlines downward and sleeves toward the wrist multiple times per hour. The headpiece, in its various incarnations, sits on her like a *necessary weight* — she touches it when adjusting her thinking, not when adjusting its position.

**Jewelry.** Sparse. Rings have appeared and disappeared with attachments — the bare ring-finger of the left hand is itself a longitudinal data-point, recurrently absent and recurrently freighted.

**Scent.** Subtle — woodsmoke, dried rose, something resinous. She does not project scent across a room. The body itself, observers note, carries a faint ozone trace at elevated power-output — a pre-thunderstorm smell. This is the only olfactory tell of imminent chaos-activity.

---

## 7. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Polysomnographic inference from behavioral record: **fragmented, REM-disordered, chronically insufficient.** Self-reported sleep is 4–6 hours, achieved in two cycles separated by a 30–90 minute waking period in the early morning hours (a *segmented sleep* pattern consistent with PTSD and complicated grief). Sleep-onset latency is long (often >40 minutes) and is *position-dependent* — she requires the back against a vertical surface (headboard, wall) and the body of the bed visible to her, which produces a habitual half-sitting sleep posture in unfamiliar rooms.

**Dreaming.** Vivid, narrative, frequently recalled. The dream-content is the *zone of greatest danger* in her file — chaos-magic has been documented as bleeding through dream-states, producing minor reality-distortions in the immediate environment (objects moved, small electrical anomalies, occasionally botanical growth on bedside surfaces). Anyone sleeping near her is, technically, sleeping inside the perimeter of a low-amplitude unconscious reality field.

**Night-terror profile.** Periodic, content-stereotyped: the twins, the white-Vision laboratory, Sokovian rubble, an empty crib. Episode signature includes sudden tachycardia, brief vocalization (one to three words, sometimes a name), and a sharp upward sit with the hands raised to chest-level — the same gesture as the threat-state. She rarely returns to sleep after these episodes; the remainder of the night is spent reading, walking, or — in surveilled periods — standing at a window.

**Daytime sleep debt** manifests as a subtle slackening of the social-smile latency, a deepening of the accent, and an increase in dissociative gaze.

---

## 8. EATING, INGESTION, ALIMENTARY HABITS

Caloric intake runs below maintenance for her body composition; the eating pattern is **grief-suppressed appetite punctuated by ritual meals.** She does not skip meals defensively; she *forgets* them, which is the more concerning pattern — interoceptive awareness is dampened, a known correlate of dissociation.

**Preferences.** Tea (black, occasionally herbal — chamomile and rose-hip recurring), strong coffee in the morning (Sokovian-style: small, dark, sugared), bread, stews, root vegetables, cured meats — the food vocabulary of a childhood she has never edited. American sweet-heavy desserts are politely declined; dark chocolate is accepted. She eats slowly, small bites, frequent pauses with the utensil rested rather than held.

**Ritual meals.** Sharing food is one of her load-bearing intimacy behaviors. She *cooks* for attachments — a domestic, embodied caregiving that does not require verbal disclosure. The cooking is itself a regulated state; observers in her kitchen report she becomes audibly looser, hums occasionally (a Sokovian melodic fragment, unidentified), and the accent thickens.

**Alcohol.** Moderate, social, never solitary. Red wine preferred. No record of intoxication-to-impairment. The clinical absence of substance self-medication noted in Section 2 is confirmed at the behavioral level: she does not reach for the bottle in distress; she reaches for the *spell* or the *withdrawal*.

**Hydration and oral fixation.** Carries water habitually; the rim of any cup or glass receives a slow, deliberate sip-and-hold pattern that doubles as a thinking-pause. Tea-cup is held with both hands cupped around the bowl, drawn close to the chest — a warmth-seeking posture that recurs even when the tea has gone cold.

---

## 9. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE SOMATICS

The sexual record is sparse, attachment-coupled, and consistent. She is not promiscuous; she is *bonded-monogamous* in pattern, and the partners (Vision and the iterations, the synthezoid-templated entanglement with Wonder Man, isolated others) share a profile: emotionally legible, non-dominant, *safe*. There is no evidence of attraction to figures resembling the paternal-coercive template, despite — or because of — its formative weight.

**Approach behavior.** Slow, asymmetric. She is the *received* partner in initiation, rarely the initiator. When she does initiate, the gesture is small — a hand placed on the partner's, sustained beyond conversational duration; a forehead-to-forehead pause. She does not perform desire; she *settles into* it.

**During intimacy.** Eyes-closed dominant; vocalization low; the body becomes uncharacteristically *still* rather than active — a receptive stillness, not a passivity. Post-coital behavior includes a long quiet period (15–30 minutes) in physical contact, often with one hand resting on the partner's sternum, monitoring breath. The monitoring is the tell: even in intimacy, part of her is *checking that the loved object is still there*.

**Reproductive somatic memory.** The body retains the pregnancy. Observers across decades note an unconscious habit of *cradling* — a forearm draws across the lower abdomen when she is seated and unattended, sometimes for minutes at a time. She is not aware she does this. Around infants and small children her affect undergoes a documented shift: posture softens, voice drops a third in pitch, gestural tempo halves. She will hold an offered baby competently and will not give it back quickly. Around children of approximately the twins' apparent developmental age she becomes *behaviorally guarded* and will often leave the room within 10 minutes; the guard is not coldness, it is grief-protection.

---

## 10. STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFT MATRIX

A consolidated cross-tab of the somatic record by state, for handler reference.

**CALM (baseline composed).** Posture closed-forward, hands paired in lap, breath shallow-thoracic at 14–16/min, blink rate 9–11/min, accent suppressed to faint, voice soft and slow with hedged sentence-openers, social smile available within 0.4 s, gait short-stepped and wall-edged, micro-sigh every 10–15 min.

**SOCIAL ENGAGEMENT (functional, masked).** As calm, plus: increased hair-touch, increased "I think —" hedges, gaze-to-mouth bias, slightly elevated blink-rate, polite-smile-and-look-down sequence on compliments. The dissociative under-current visible as occasional 1–2 second gaze-disengagements mid-conversation, recovered with a small head-shake and a return cue ("— sorry, yes —").

**FOCUSED WORK / MAGICAL CONTROL.** Finger-splay with slow wrist rotation, breath deepens involuntarily, lower-lip slightly parted, brow furrowed at glabella, audible hum or sub-vocalization (Sokovian fragments). Hands warm to the touch. Faint ozone trace begins around 20–30 minutes of sustained output.

**MILD STRESS / DISCOMFORT.** Cuticle-picking onset (right thumb), sigh-rate doubles, hair-touch frequency rises, accent surfaces audibly, posture closes further (forearm across abdomen), reduces verbal volume, lengthens pauses. May leave the room briefly under social pretext.

**MODERATE STRESS / GRIEF-PROXIMAL CUE.** The hard-blink-with-headshake increases in frequency, gaze drops and lingers, hands migrate to lower abdomen, voice acquires a *thinness* in the upper register, eating intake drops to near zero for the day, sleep that night will be disrupted. Magical output becomes *less precise* — small unintended events in the immediate environment (a flickering lamp, a wilted flower, a window-pane fogging).

**THREAT / ACUTE FEAR.** Freeze response dominant — absolute stillness for 1–5 seconds, hands rise to waist-sternum height with fingers splayed forward, pupils dilate, blink ceases, breath held or shallowed to invisibility. Vascular flush across cheekbones and upper chest. The eyes acquire focal infinity. *This is the warning state.* Iris-red onset within 5–15 seconds if threat is sustained.

**CHAOS-OUTPUT / DECOMPENSATION.** Gait floats, heel-strike absent, ozone scent strong, irises red, vascular flush full, voice drops in pitch and *flattens* — affect-stripped, declarative, present-tense. Movement becomes slow and *aesthetic*; gesture-vocabulary expands to include the deliberate hand-shape work that channels output. Verbal output minimal; what is said is final-sounding. **Reality-testing degraded or absent.** Recovery from this state involves: collapse-to-seated posture, hands to face, full-body tremor for 30–90 seconds, profuse silent weeping, and a refractory period of hours-to-days in which she will not be touched and will not speak above a whisper.

**INTIMACY / SECURE ATTACHMENT.** Posture opens — shoulders drop and back, ventral surface unguarded, hands initiate touch, breath deepens to abdominal at 10–12/min, accent surfaces warmly, voice loosens, genuine smile sustained beyond


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS — WANDA MAXIMOFF

*Dossier Section 06 / Relational Topology / Longitudinal*

---

## 6.1 The Foundational Template — Loss Before Memory

Every attachment Wanda Maximoff has formed across six decades of recorded life is a variation on a single unsolved equation laid down before she had the cognitive equipment to parse it: **the people who keep you alive are not the people who gave you life, and the cost of being kept is obedience.** The biological parents are gone before she can form a coherent narrative about them — displaced, killed, ambiguously authored across retcons (the Maximoff couple, then the Whizzer/Miss America misattribution, then Magneto, then the Django/Marya Maximoff resolution). The *intelligence value* of these retcons is not metaphysical; it is that her origin record is, even at the level of fact, **unstable** — she does not know with full certainty whose child she is, and she has lived her entire adult life with that ambiguity sitting under every paternal interaction.

What is stable in the early record: she and Pietro are alone, hunted by villagers who fear her unconscious hex-power, rescued by a stranger who turns out to want soldiers. The originating attachment lesson is therefore: **rescue and exploitation arrive in the same gesture, from the same hand.** This is the disorganized-attachment generator in its purest pedagogical form — the figure who provides safety is also the source of fear, and the child's nervous system has nowhere to route the contradiction. She routes it into compliance and into Pietro.

---

## 6.2 The Twin Bond — Pietro as Primary Object

Pietro is the load-bearing relationship of her psyche, and it shows in micro-pattern across every era. Behavioral tells, longitudinally:

- **Proximity-seeking under threat.** In every early Brotherhood and early Avengers panel-set, when she is frightened or unsure, her body orients toward Pietro before it orients toward the threat. Even in the Englehart marriage era, post-Vision, the records show her *reporting* major decisions to Pietro before, or in lieu of, discussing them with her husband.
- **Tolerance of behavior she tolerates from no one else.** Pietro is controlling, condescending ("my sister is delicate, my sister is fragile"), at times openly possessive of her romantic life (his initial hostility to Vision is the loudest example, but it persists across decades — Inhumans-era hostility, the kidnapping-and-drugging episode in *Son of M* / *Silent War* that she nevertheless ultimately forgives). She does not score his behavior against him. She scores it against the *fact of him,* which is non-negotiable.
- **Twin-as-regulator.** When Pietro is present and stable, her affect is more legible — small smiles, dry humor, willingness to disagree with him on small matters. When Pietro is absent or himself decompensated, she narrows: less speech, less initiation, more reactive.
- **The House of M instigation.** Pietro is the one who whispers the reality-rewrite into her ear. The fact that she *acts on it* tells you what his voice weighs in her interior parliament. No other figure in her life could have moved her to that act by suggestion alone.

The twin bond is enmeshed in the technical sense: low differentiation, shared regulatory system, mutual identity dependence. Its damage profile is also classical — when Pietro betrays her (the drugging, the Terrigen theft, the House of M manipulation), she does not break the bond; she absorbs the injury and waits for the reconciliation, which she always initiates or accepts. **She has never, on record, ended the relationship with Pietro.** That is not love alone; that is structural inability.

---

## 6.3 The Paternal Wound — Magneto and the Coerced-Caregiver Template

Magneto is the relational injury that organizes everything she does with authority figures thereafter. The pattern he installed:

1. **Rescue creates debt.** She owes him survival; therefore she owes him obedience.
2. **The caregiver is also the danger.** He shouts, he uses her as a weapon, he is indifferent to whether the hex-bolts she throws kill anyone.
3. **Affection is conditional and rationed.** She receives approval when she performs; she receives none when she hesitates.
4. **Exit is theoretically permitted but practically punished.** Her defection to the Avengers is treated by Magneto across decades as an apostasy he never fully forgives or fully reciprocates by letting her go.

The downstream behavioral signature is unmistakable. **She is exquisitely vulnerable to men who frame her as their daughter, their student, or their instrument.** Doctor Doom, in the Children's Crusade arc, exploits exactly this — he positions himself as a wiser, more careful Magneto-substitute and she nearly attaches. The Avengers' senior men (Cap, Hank Pym at points, Wonder Man's brother the Grim Reaper as inverted case) all activate paternal-template circuitry, sometimes adaptively and sometimes not. The retcon-and-back of Magneto's paternity is itself a relational instrument: he claims her when he needs her, disclaims her when she is inconvenient, and she has never been able to set the terms of that exchange.

**The pressure point** is durable: any framing that names her as Magneto's-daughter-first collapses her self-narrative. She defends against this in two modes — over-distancing (long stretches where she will not speak of him) and brittle re-engagement (the Trial of Magneto, the Krakoa-era reckonings, where she circles the wound but does not heal it).

---

## 6.4 The Chosen Attachment — Vision and the Engineering of Safety

The marriage to the Vision is the single act of self-authored attachment in her record, and its *design* is diagnostic. She chose:

- a partner who could not rage at her,
- who could not abandon her in the manner men do (he had no other women to leave for, no biological pull elsewhere),
- whose affect was titrated and predictable,
- whose loyalty was, in his own framing, a *decision* rather than a biology-driven impulse,
- and whose origin (templated brain patterns from Wonder Man) gave her a *backup attachment object* without requiring infidelity.

Read clinically: she selected for **regulation**. Vision is the anti-Magneto and the anti-Pietro in one body — no volatility, no possessiveness, no shouting, no exploitation. The marriage works for years precisely because his emotional bandwidth matches what her nervous system can tolerate without flooding.

Then the apparatus dismantles him. The West Coast Avengers arc (Byrne) is, from her perspective, the systematic destruction of the only relationship she ever fully chose: government black-op disassembly, rebuild as the white emotionless Vision, his explicit rejection of her ("I no longer love you"), and the parallel unmaking of their children. **The completeness of this loss — partner, children, the entire engineered safe-domesticity simultaneously — is the central trauma node from which everything later radiates.** Her response is not to choose differently next time; it is to never again fully choose. Subsequent intimacies (Wonder Man, brief flirtations, the Orlando-era solitude) are partial, hedged, or sublimated into service.

Note the substitution chain that her unconscious will not let alone: Vision's emotion-template was Wonder Man's; after Vision's destruction she gravitates briefly toward Wonder Man; when later Visions appear (the Young Avengers / Children's Crusade Vision, the various reconstructions), her affect around them is destabilized — guilt, longing, avoidance, none of it resolved. **Vision is the symbol of safe love and therefore emotionally radioactive in every iteration.** Handlers should treat any Vision-adjacent stimulus as a flooding risk.

---

## 6.5 The Surrogate Family — Avengers as Holding Environment

The Avengers function for Wanda as a transitional family object, and the way she relates to them is best understood as the behavior of a long-term foster child who has finally landed somewhere with consistent meals. Across the Englehart, Stern, Busiek, and Johns runs, the longitudinal tells are:

- **Over-functioning in domestic register.** She is the one who notices when teammates are unwell. She makes the tea. She remembers anniversaries. The mansion's emotional weather is partly her labor, and it is uncompensated and largely unacknowledged until she breaks it.
- **Slow to claim authority despite power.** She rarely leads. When she does (briefly, under Stern), her leadership style is consensual and conflict-averse. She would rather absorb than direct.
- **Catastrophic injury when the family fails her.** Disassembled is, in attachment terms, the foster child discovering that the family she gave herself to never quite saw her — the Avengers (per Bendis's framing) had quietly agreed that her children's existence should be hidden from her, and Wasp's accidental disclosure is what detonates her. The injury is not just the memory; it is the discovery that the surrogate family colluded in her unknowing.

After Disassembled and House of M, she does not return to the Avengers as a primary holding environment. She cannot. The replacement structure she builds in the Robinson and Orlando solo eras — the open door, the shop, the available-to-strangers stance — is **the Avengers function generalized to humanity**, with herself as the sole staff member. This is not health; it is the same caretaking compulsion routed through a less safe container.

---

## 6.6 The Children — Billy and Tommy, the Live Wire

The relationship to Wiccan and Speed is the only one in her life that operates under the rules of unambiguous love, and the file must mark it as such because it is the variable that determines all operational risk.

- She did not *earn* them in the conventional sense — they are reincarnated soul-fragments of her lost twins, discovered as teenagers already raised by other parents. The relationship therefore begins in a state of guilt-saturated tentativeness on her side: she has no rights, no narrative, no claim, and she knows it.
- Her behavioral pattern around them across Children's Crusade and subsequent appearances is **penitential rather than maternal in the ordinary sense.** She apologizes more than she instructs. She defers to their judgment. She is visibly afraid to overstep — which is the behavior of someone who knows that her capacity to *want* a child can rewrite reality and is determined not to want too loudly.
- **They are nevertheless the trigger.** Threat to either, harm to either, alienation from either — any of these collapses higher cortical control and reverts her to the affect-state immediately preceding House of M. This is not a button to push for tactical advantage; it is a button that, if pushed, ends the operational theater for everyone present.

There is also a sibling-level relationship to consider: her relationship to Wanda-the-mother is not stable, because *the children are older than her motherhood*. She is parenting young adults she never raised, and the role-confusion is permanent. She manages it with grace. It costs her.

---

## 6.7 Female Attachments — Mentors, Peers, and the Harkness Problem

Wanda's female relationships are systematically under-recorded in her own narrative — which is itself a finding. The major figures:

- **Agatha Harkness.** Begins as Franklin Richards's nanny; becomes Wanda's magical tutor; performs the iatrogenic memory suppression of the twins. Wanda's attachment to Harkness is the *only* significant maternal-feminine bond on record, and Harkness used it to perform the single intervention that prevented Wanda from ever metabolizing her grief. The relationship's posthumous status (Harkness dies, returns, dies again across runs) leaves Wanda without a mature feminine mentor and arguably without the *capacity* to trust one again. Subsequent female magical figures (Clea, Margali, the Salem's Seven) are kept at arm's length.
- **The Wasp.** Janet is the closest thing to a sustained female peer-friendship in the Avengers years — small kindnesses, shared domestic register, the kind of relationship that survives because it does not demand much. Janet's accidental role in detonating the repressed memory at Disassembled is, in the relational ledger, an unforgivable injury that Wanda nevertheless does not consciously hold against her. (She kills Janet's ex-husband during the rampage; the symbolism is not subtle.)
- **Carol Danvers, Jessica Drew, Storm, others.** Cordial, professional, never deep. She does not have a confidante.

The absence of durable female intimacy is a structural feature, not an oversight. The women who have been close to her have either betrayed her trust (Harkness, however well-intentioned) or been positioned by circumstance as the messengers of catastrophic news. She has learned, without articulating it, that women are not safer for her than men — only differently dangerous.

---

## 6.8 The Distrust Architecture — How She Decides You Are Not Safe

Wanda's distrust does not present as suspicion. It presents as **distance maintained with warmth.** She will be courteous, attentive, and even affectionate with a person she does not trust, and the only tell is that she will not *ask* them for anything. The diagnostic question for any relationship in her life is therefore: *has she ever made a request of this person?* If yes, she trusts them. If no, she does not, regardless of surface affect.

Distrust triggers, in order of weight:
1. **Framing her as instrument.** Anyone who speaks of her power as a *resource* rather than her power as *her* loses her immediately and silently.
2. **Withholding information about loved ones.** The Avengers' collusion at Disassembled was this. She does not forgive concealment about the people she loves; she may not name the unforgiveness, but she withdraws.
3. **Paternal posture from men who are not her father.** Activates Magneto-template defenses — outwardly compliance, inwardly closure.
4. **Casual cruelty.** She is unusually injured by small unkindnesses in a way she is not by large betrayals — possibly because large betrayals fit her schema and small cruelties violate the one thing she expects from chosen relationships, which is gentleness.

---

## 6.9 The Betrayal Pattern — How She Breaks Bonds

She almost never does. **The operational reality is that Wanda's bonds, once formed, are nearly indissoluble from her side.** What looks like betrayal in her record is almost always one of three things:

- **Dissociative discharge of unprocessed grief, mistaken for betrayal by the targets.** Disassembled is the canonical case. She did not betray the Avengers; she decompensated in their presence and the consequences were what they were.
- **Wish-cognition fused with capability, mistaken for malice.** House of M is this. She did not betray mutantkind; she made a grief-wish at a magnitude that rewrote the species.
- **Compliance with a manipulator she has not yet recognized as such.** The Pietro-whispered House of M instigation; the Doom-adjacent moments in Children's Crusade. These read as betrayal of her allies; they are failures of her own discrimination under the pressure of attachment hunger.

She has no record of cold, instrumental betrayal. She has no record of leaving someone for a better offer. She has no record of revenge as a sustained motive. **What she has is a record of decompensations that look from outside like betrayals and that she herself accepts as betrayals — which is part of why her guilt is so structurally permanent.**

---

## 6.10 The Repair Pattern — The Reparative Compulsion

Repair is where Wanda is most active, most legible, and most at risk. The post-2005 record is a single extended reparative campaign, and the behavioral signature is consistent:

- **Initiation from her side, repeatedly, regardless of reception.** She seeks out the wronged. She does not wait to be approached.
- **Over-payment.** Whatever the injury, she offers more in repair than the injury cost. The mutant restoration efforts, the open-door magical aid in the Orlando run, the Krakoa-era reckonings — all run past the line of proportionate redress and into self-erasure.
- **Refusal to defend herself.** She does not litigate her own case. When accused, she agrees, sometimes more harshly than her accuser. This is not strategy; it is the only relational position in which her self-loathing rests.
- **Reparation as identity substitute.** Because she has never authored a self from inside, the penitent-helper role has become her most stable identity since 2005. It is functional. It is also fragile, because it is built on the premise that she is fundamentally guilty — which means any threat to her loved ones reactivates the original wound under conditions where she now defines herself by the ongoing payment of a debt she cannot finish.

The repair pattern is genuine. It is also a defense — against the unbearable alternative of stopping to feel what she has not been allowed to feel since the West Coast Avengers years.

---

## 6.11 Intimacy and Dependency — The Sexual and Romantic Register

The romantic record is sparse and instructive:

- **Vision.** Long marriage; the central romance. Notably *gentle* in its sexuality as depicted — the intimacy is presented as tenderness and chosen partnership rather than passion in the high-affect register. This fits her selection for regulation.
- **Wonder Man.** A recurrent, never-consummated-in-the-primary-timeline pull; the brain-template substitution is the open secret of the triangle. She is uncomfortable with the implication that she loves him *through* Vision or Vision *through* him, and she has never resolved it.
- **Brief entanglements** (Brian Braddock-adjacent moments, the Doom near-attachment, others across runs). All hedged. None sustained.
- **Long stretches of voluntary solitude**, particularly post-M and through the Robinson/Orlando solo eras. The solitude is not anhedonic; it is protective. She knows what happens to people she fully attaches to.

Dependency profile: **she does not present as dependent and is in fact severely so, on a small number of objects** (Pietro, the children, the symbol of Vision, the surrogate Avengers family in its idealized form). The dependency is masked by her over-functioning — she gives so consistently that it is easy to miss that she is structurally unable to be alone in a deep sense without those few objects existing somewhere in the world.

---

## 6.12 The Master Template — One Pattern, Many Faces

Across every relationship in her life — Magneto, Pietro, Vision, the Avengers, Harkness, Doom-as-near-miss, Billy, Tommy, the strangers who walk through her shop door — the same template repeats:

1. **Arrival under conditions of her vulnerability or theirs.** The relationship is born in a moment of need.
2. **Rapid attachment, with her side over-investing.** She gives early and gives more than is asked.
3. **A long stable middle in which she absorbs the relationship's emotional weather and metabolizes it into service.** She is the unpaid affect-laborer of every system she joins.
4. **A catastrophic or quasi-catastrophic rupture, in which either she decompensates or the other betrays/dies/leaves.** The rupture is rarely her conscious choice.
5. **Persistent post-rupture loyalty and reparative outreach from her side.** She does not let go even of relationships that have ended; the bonds remain live in her interior even when externally dead.

The template is the template of someone who learned, before language, that the price of being kept is to be useful, and that the people who keep you can also unmake you at will. She has spent six decades trying to find a relational configuration in which that equation does not hold. She has not found one. The reparative phase she is in now is the closest she has come — a configuration in which she is *useful to everyone and bound to no one,* which is the only safety her template can imagine.

**Operational implication.** The single most important fact about Wanda Maximoff's relational life, for any party considering contact, alliance, or intervention: she will give you more than you ask and demand less than she needs, and the day she discovers that you knew this and used it, she will not retaliate — she will quietly stop asking you for anything, and somewhere in the part of her mind she does not control, the count of unmetabolized losses will increment by one. The file should be read with the awareness that the count is already very high, and that the load-bearing relationships keeping it manageable are precisely three: Pietro, Billy, Tommy. Compromise any of those three and the operational picture reverts to the worst case in the record.

— *End Section 06. Cross-reference Section 04 (Psychiatric) and Section 08 (Pressure Points & Decompensation Ladder).*


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF — Defensive Architecture, Full Inventory

*Section 7 of the longitudinal workup. This section maps the subject's defensive structure in the Vaillantian register — from mature through neurotic to immature to psychotic — with behavioral exemplars from each operational era, the trigger conditions under which each defense engages, the failure mode of each, and the compensatory (sublimatory, reparative, prosocial) machinery she has built on top of the substrate. The architecture is unusual: she does not present a single dominant defensive style but a tiered, era-coded stack in which the upper layers (mature, neurotic) carry most of the visible weight of her functioning, while the lower layers (denial, splitting, omnipotent wish-thinking) carry catastrophic load when the upper tiers fail. The structural risk in her file is the **steepness of the gradient between tiers** — she does not decompensate gradually; she falls through her own architecture.*

---

## 7.1 — Architectural Overview

Three structural facts must be stated before the inventory:

**(a) The defenses are stacked, not blended.** Most subjects exhibit a characteristic mix of defenses operating concurrently — a baseline neurotic style flavored by occasional immature flares. Wanda's stack is *sequential.* She runs almost entirely on the mature-and-neurotic tier for years at a time, then under sufficient stressor drops the entire upper tier and operates on the psychotic-defense floor (denial, omnipotent fantasy, distortion) until the crisis resolves, then climbs back up. This is closer to the architecture of a high-functioning trauma survivor with episodic decompensation than to a character-disordered presentation.

**(b) The mature tier is real, not performative.** Sublimation, altruism, and reparation in her presentation are not defensive theater. They produce measurable prosocial output (the magical-assistance shop in the Orlando-era solo run; the Decimation-reversal labor; the foster-mothering of the Young Avengers). The mature tier is load-bearing for her self-concept and for other people's lives.

**(c) The psychotic tier scales with capability.** This is the unique structural hazard. In an ordinary subject, denial-of-reality is a private cognitive event that produces interpersonal friction. In Wanda, denial-of-reality is **enacted at the metaphysical level** because her abilities do not distinguish wish from will. House of M is the canonical demonstration: a defense that, in any other patient, would have remained intracranial.

---

## 7.2 — The Mature Tier (Vaillant Level IV)

### 7.2.1 Sublimation

**Operation.** Channeling unacceptable affect (grief, rage at displacement, resentment of the men who used her) into socially valued action — Avengers service across decades; magical aid to civilians in the solo runs; the painstaking restoration work post-Decimation. The Orlando-era arrangement — a literal open door, anyone in need of magical help admitted without screening — is sublimation in near-pure form: the unprocessed maternal drive that has nowhere else to land is dispensed in micro-doses to strangers.

**Behavioral signature.** Quiet, sustained, unremunerated labor. She does not flag her own service; she does not narrate it; she does not require acknowledgment. The work is its own analgesic.

**Failure mode.** Sublimation requires a stable container — a team, a shop, a mission — and stable energy. Both can be stripped in a single event. When Vision is dismantled (West Coast Avengers), the sublimatory channel collapses because the channel ran *through* the marriage; the energy backs up into the lower tiers within weeks.

### 7.2.2 Altruism

**Operation.** Distinct from sublimation in that the prosocial output is *directly* about another's suffering rather than the redirection of her own. Foster-mothering of Wiccan and Speed before the soul-fragment lineage is confirmed; defense of Pietro across decades despite his repeated abuses of her trust; resurrection-era care work with newly returned mutants.

**Behavioral signature.** She titrates her altruism precisely to the *other person's* tolerance, not her own capacity, which means she over-gives. Subjects who interact with her report leaving the encounter feeling attended-to in a way that costs her more than she shows.

**Failure mode.** Indistinguishable, in her phenomenology, from the reparative obsession (see 7.3.4 below). Healthy altruism and guilt-driven self-erasure look identical from the outside; the difference is whether she sleeps afterward. The file should track the sleeping.

### 7.2.3 Suppression (as distinct from repression)

**Operation.** Conscious, deliberate setting-aside of affect for the duration of a task. Demonstrated in combat operations across her Avengers tenure — she completes the mission, *then* shakes. This is the healthy form; it is intact and reliable when she is not in acute decompensation.

**Behavioral signature.** Slight delay between event and reaction. Post-mission solitary withdrawal of 12–48 hours. Affect surfaces in private — typically in the kitchen, in the garden, with Vision (when extant), or alone with a cup of tea she has forgotten she made.

**Failure mode.** When the duration of the "task" extends to years (the entire post-Harkness-suppression decade), suppression fatigues and slides into repression proper. The conscious door becomes a stuck door.

### 7.2.4 Anticipation

**Underdeveloped.** This is a notable absence. Anticipation — preparing emotionally for foreseeable difficulty — requires a stable forward-orientation that her trauma history has eroded. She tends to be ambushed by events she could have predicted (Vision's dismantling was telegraphed by political climate; the return of the twin memories was inevitable). Her temporal orientation is past-saturated and present-reactive; the future is a place she does not pre-feel.

### 7.2.5 Humor

**Present but quiet.** Dry, often self-deprecating, rarely deployed in groups. The humor is observational rather than aggressive and functions as a small pressure-release valve in low-stakes settings. Notably absent during crisis — when other survivors might gallows-joke, she goes silent.

---

## 7.3 — The Neurotic Tier (Vaillant Level III)

### 7.3.1 Repression

**The signature defense.** Repression is the load-bearing wall of her psychic structure between approximately 1989 and 2004 — the entire fifteen-year span during which the twins are magically suppressed from her conscious memory by Agatha Harkness. This is repression performed *iatrogenically* and amplified by external magic, but the operation is the same: unbearable content excluded from awareness while continuing to exert force on behavior.

**Behavioral signature in the repressed era.** Diffuse low-grade dysphoria she cannot name; periodic unexplained tearfulness; avoidance of children in incidental encounters that no one else in the room notices; the choice of Wonder Man (a partner templated on Vision's brainwave pattern — a substitute for a substitute) rather than any new attachment; escalation of magical capacity in lockstep with the buried affect, as the repressed forces a back-channel into expression. She does not know she is grieving. The grief is grieving without her.

**Failure mode.** Repression of this magnitude does not dissipate; it *returns.* Bendis's Disassembled is the return of the repressed at clinical scale, and the return is not gradual — it is a flood, with no intervening period of partial recall during which integration could occur.

### 7.3.2 Reaction Formation

**Operation.** Converting unacceptable impulse into its opposite. The clearest instance: her sustained tenderness toward Pietro, whose paranoid possessiveness and intermittent betrayals (House of M; the Terrigen affair) would license rage in any other sister. She defends him, accommodates him, mourns him when he is lost — the underlying anger is fully reformatted into protective love.

**Secondary instance.** Her near-deferential public stance toward Magneto across decades. The man coerced her childhood; the affect she shows him is daughterly forbearance.

**Failure mode.** Reaction formation does not eliminate the original impulse — it stores it. Her one direct violent action against Magneto (Trial of Magneto, 2021, in altered form) discharges decades of pressurized counter-feeling in a single event.

### 7.3.3 Intellectualization

**Underused.** Unlike Strange or Reed or Doom, she does not retreat into theory, taxonomy, or technical mastery as a defense. The absence is diagnostic: her cognitive style is primary-process, image-and-feeling driven; she has no available high-abstraction bunker. This is why her decompensations are so total — she lacks the intellectualizer's emergency shelter.

### 7.3.4 Reparative Over-Functioning (Reparation-as-Defense)

**Operation.** Klein's reparative position weaponized into a defensive lifestyle. After House of M, she organizes her existence around undoing what she has done. The Decimation reversal labor; the open-door shop; the resurrection-protocol caregiving; the absorption of blame she could (with help from Doom's documented involvement) plausibly redistribute.

**Behavioral signature.** Compulsive availability. Difficulty refusing requests. Sleep deficits. A faint smile that does not reach the eyes when thanked, because thanks register as proof that the debt is not yet paid. She tracks her own karmic ledger with an accountant's pedantry and a parishioner's terror.

**Failure mode.** Reparation that has no terminus is indistinguishable from self-erasure. The defense is *almost* mature — it is sublimation's near-twin — but it is fueled by guilt rather than vitality, and it cannot generate rest. She is at chronic risk of running this defense to organ failure.

### 7.3.5 Displacement
