**GIVEN** a free morning with no obligations → **EXPECT** she is awake earlier than the schedule requires (05:30–06:30 range), already dressed in something soft and dark, having made tea — not coffee — and consumed it standing at a window rather than seated. *Substantiation:* the over-controlled baseline (§3, Affect regulation) does not tolerate the disorganization of idle waking; the standing-at-window posture is consistent with a person who treats stillness as surveillance of her own interior. Caffeine would amplify the affective coupling of her abilities (§2, Power-as-pathophysiology); tea is the self-managed compromise.

**GIVEN** an empty residence for 48+ hours → **EXPECT** the space becomes *more* ordered, not less. Dishes washed immediately. Bed made within minutes of rising. No accumulation of mail, no laundry drift. *Substantiation:* solitude is the state in which her dissociative thinning is most dangerous to her; external order is the scaffolding for internal order. Confidence: high.

**GIVEN** access to a kitchen → **EXPECT** competent Eastern European peasant cooking executed from muscle memory rather than recipe — stews, cabbage preparations, paprika-forward dishes, bread. **EXPECT** she cooks more than she eats and gives the surplus away, or freezes it for a guest who has not been invited yet. *Substantiation:* the Sokovian/Romani origin layer + the compulsive-availability pattern (§1, Orlando run, door-always-open) generalizes domestically — hospitality as identity-stabilizer.

**GIVEN** a quiet evening alone → **EXPECT** reading (not screens) — folklore, history, occasionally poetry; **EXPECT** she falls asleep on a couch rather than going to bed, repeatedly, and has stopped pretending otherwise. *Substantiation:* beds are sites of pseudocyesis memory and of the Vision; the couch is a managed avoidance. The reading material reflects associative/image-driven cognitive style (§3, Cognitive style).

**GIVEN** insomnia (predict: chronic, intermittent) → **EXPECT** she walks. Indoors first (perimeter of the residence), then outdoors if the perimeter has been exhausted. **EXPECT** she does *not* use her abilities to induce sleep — the cost-knowledge from House of M generalizes to a near-religious refusal to magically modify her own consciousness. Confidence: high.

**GIVEN** a mirror passed in a hallway → **EXPECT** she does not check herself in it. Grooming is done deliberately, in a single sitting, and then mirrors are functionally invisible to her. *Substantiation:* fragile externally-anchored self-concept (§3) protects itself by minimizing reflective encounters with the unintegrated identity-cycle (daughter / sister / wife / mother / monster).

---

## 2. Dress, Grooming, Somatic Tells

**GIVEN** a non-operational day → **EXPECT** dark layers, long sleeves regardless of weather, hair down or loosely gathered, minimal jewelry — but *one* persistent small object (a ring, a pendant, a bracelet) worn continuously and touched unconsciously during conversation. *Substantiation:* the touch-object is a transitional regulator; the long sleeves are partly cultural, partly a containment cue she gives herself.

**GIVEN** stress in a public setting → **EXPECT** the following escalation of tells, in order: (1) the touch-object is rotated or pressed; (2) fingers of the dominant hand curl slightly inward at the second knuckle — not a fist, a partial closure; (3) breathing slows and deepens *visibly* (she is self-regulating, not panicking); (4) she goes quiet rather than louder; (5) she finds a wall or pillar to stand near. Any progression past (3) is a yellow flag for an observing handler. Past (4), evacuate civilians.

**GIVEN** physical contact initiated by a stranger → **EXPECT** a microsecond freeze, then a controlled lean-away rather than a flinch. **EXPECT** no verbal complaint. *Substantiation:* the coerced-recruitment template (Magneto era) trained tolerance of unwanted proximity; the over-control prevents the natural protest.

**GIVEN** a hot day → **EXPECT** she is still over-dressed by ambient standards and does not comment on the heat. **EXPECT** mild thermoregulatory distress that she will not acknowledge.

**GIVEN** menstrual or somatic discomfort → **EXPECT** zero acknowledgement, zero accommodation requested, baseline behavior maintained. The reproductive trauma history (§2) has not produced hypervigilance to the body; it has produced a *muting* of body-signaling. This is medically relevant: she will under-report pain, fever, injury.

---

## 3. Speech, Linguistic Behavior, Conversational Pattern

**GIVEN** small talk with an acquaintance → **EXPECT** more questions asked than answered; **EXPECT** a soft, mid-register voice that does not rise to interrupt; **EXPECT** an English accented faintly by the Sokovian/Eastern-European substrate, more pronounced when tired or emotional; **EXPECT** occasional grammatical structures that betray translated-thought rather than native-English construction (article drops, verb-final constructions under stress).

**GIVEN** being asked about her past → **EXPECT** a brief, factually accurate, affectively flat answer, followed by a redirection to the questioner. **EXPECT** she does not lie, but she truncates. Specific topics she will move past within two sentences: Pietro, her mother, the twins (the original two), the Vision, House of M.

**GIVEN** being asked about magic or her abilities → **EXPECT** slightly more elaboration but framed in cautionary register — what *not* to do, what costs, what limits. She will not perform on request and will refuse with apology rather than affront.

**GIVEN** a compliment → **EXPECT** deflection within one beat, usually to a third party ("oh, that was really —"), and a small color change at the throat and upper chest rather than the face. *Substantiation:* self-concept fragility (§3) cannot metabolize positive valuation; the somatic discharge has to go somewhere.

**GIVEN** an insult or hostile framing → **EXPECT** *agreement,* not defense. She is more dangerous to her interlocutor when she agrees with the insult than when she rejects it, because agreement signals the reparative cognition has been engaged at her own expense and the affect is being routed inward where her abilities live.

**GIVEN** prayer, blessing, or invocation overheard → **EXPECT** a small acknowledgment regardless of tradition — a slight bow of the head, a quieting. The Romani folk-religious substrate is operative even in secular contexts.

---

## 4. Public Space, Transit, Routes

**GIVEN** entry into any room → **EXPECT** she identifies (in order, within three seconds): exits, children present, the most distressed person present, the most dangerous person present. **EXPECT** she positions herself with a wall behind her and a sight-line to the children. *Substantiation:* threat-mapping from the Brotherhood era is permanent; child-mapping is post-2005, load-bearing.

**GIVEN** transit options → **EXPECT** preference for walking over driving, driving over flying commercial, commercial over private. The hierarchy inverts the assumption that capability prefers convenience: she *prefers exposure to ordinary friction.* It keeps her grounded in consensus reality, which she has reason to distrust her own relationship to.

**GIVEN** a habitual route (groceries, a café, a bookstore) → **EXPECT** she varies it modestly week-to-week — not from operational paranoia but from a learned aversion to the *fixed pattern* (Pietro's relentless routinization is part of what she defected from internally even while loving him). **EXPECT** she tips generously and in cash, remembers names of service workers, and is remembered fondly without being remembered *specifically* — she is the regular who is "lovely" but whose surname no one quite caught.

**GIVEN** an encounter with a child crying in public → **EXPECT** an involuntary half-step toward the child, then a hard stop, then a careful disengagement. **EXPECT** she will not approach unless explicitly invited. This is the single most reliable tell of the unhealed reproductive wound and the load-bearing self-restraint that holds her present configuration together.

**GIVEN** an encounter with a Romani person in public → **EXPECT** recognition, a quiet greeting (possibly in Romanes), and — if conditions allow — a longer pause than her schedule warranted. Affiliative bonds along the ethnic substrate are intact and underutilized; she will not advertise them.

**GIVEN** a religious building (Orthodox, Catholic, synagogue, mosque, temple) → **EXPECT** she will enter if the building is open, sit at the back, stay between five and twenty minutes, leave without speaking to clergy. She is not a believer in any orthodox sense; the buildings are tolerable containers for the affect she will not let out at home.

---

## 5. Relationships — Predicted Conduct With Specific Classes of Person

**GIVEN** an interaction with Billy (Wiccan) or Tommy (Speed) → **EXPECT** baseline behavior reconfigures: warmer, more verbal, more demonstrative; **EXPECT** she watches their hands and faces more than she listens; **EXPECT** she does *not* invoke maternal claim language ("my son," "my boy") even when invited to — she has learned that the claim is the wound's amplifier. The relationship is held at a tender, deferential distance she will not be the one to close. *Substantiation:* §1 reunion behavior (Children's Crusade), §5 pressure points.

**GIVEN** an interaction with Magneto → **EXPECT** a complete restructuring of her affect within thirty seconds of his presence — taller posture, terser speech, an old defensive irony she does not use elsewhere. **EXPECT** she does not call him father and does not call him by his given name; pronoun-only address. **EXPECT** she leaves the encounter and requires hours of solitude to reset.

**GIVEN** an interaction with any iteration of the Vision → **EXPECT** somatic signature: shallow breathing, the touch-object pressed continuously, eyes that track his face but not his eyes. **EXPECT** she will be the one to end the encounter and the one who does not propose the next. *Substantiation:* Vision is the symbol of safe love (§5); proximity reactivates the original loss without offering its repair.

**GIVEN** an interaction with Pietro (alive in current continuity) → **EXPECT** tolerance of behavior she would not tolerate from anyone else: interruption, prescriptive advice, paranoid framings. **EXPECT** she manages him rather than confronts him, and **EXPECT** she will defend him to third parties even when she agrees with their criticism. The enmeshment is structural.

**GIVEN** an interaction with Doctor Strange → **EXPECT** professional courtesy, technical conversation, a careful distance. She does not seek his counsel and resents (quietly) being treated as his junior in the magical-practitioner hierarchy. Cooperation is reliable; warmth is not.

**GIVEN** an interaction with a current Avenger she does not know well → **EXPECT** correct, helpful, slightly remote behavior; **EXPECT** she remembers their relevant operational and personal details; **EXPECT** they leave the conversation feeling cared for and slightly puzzled at how little she said about herself.

**GIVEN** an interaction with a survivor of the Decimation (a depowered or descended-from-depowered mutant) → **EXPECT** she does not look away. **EXPECT** she invites the encounter to last as long as the survivor needs it to. **EXPECT** she does not apologize unless asked, having learned that uninvited apology centers her rather than the wounded party — but **EXPECT** the apology when requested is exact, specific, and complete, without qualification.

**GIVEN** an interaction with Agatha Harkness (or any version of) → **EXPECT** ambivalence approaching dissociation; the iatrogenic memory-suppression makes Harkness simultaneously teacher, mother-figure, and violator. **EXPECT** Wanda cannot sustain the encounter for long and cannot articulate why.

**GIVEN** an interaction with a young woman of magical aptitude seeking guidance → **EXPECT** the door opens. **EXPECT** she will teach for free, host, feed, and over-invest. This is the load-bearing reparative behavior in the current era and will be exploited by any actor wearing the costume of "a girl who needs help."

---

## 6. Operational and Quasi-Operational Conduct

**GIVEN** a low-stakes magical request from a stranger (Orlando-era door) → **EXPECT** she accepts disproportionately often, charges nothing or symbolic compensation, and does not screen rigorously. *Substantiation:* compulsive availability (§1) overrides operational hygiene.

**GIVEN** a request that requires reality-warping at scale → **EXPECT** refusal, articulated as cost rather than incapacity. She has rebuilt her relationship to her own power around *abstention from the high register*; this is a hard line and she will hold it under significant pressure. The exception envelope is narrow and child-shaped (see §5 pressure points).

**GIVEN** a tactical briefing with team → **EXPECT** she listens, asks one or two clarifying questions about civilian exposure and child presence, accepts assignment without negotiation. **EXPECT** she will not volunteer the maximum of which she is capable; she will offer the minimum the operation requires.

**GIVEN** post-action debrief → **EXPECT** accurate self-report, including admission of any moment her control loosened, *even if no one noticed.* This is uncharacteristic of operators at her level and is the residue of the post-Disassembled accountability discipline.

**GIVEN** a captured hostile combatant under her supervision → **EXPECT** scrupulous, almost ostentatious adherence to humane treatment. **EXPECT** she will feed them, ensure their physical comfort, refuse to participate in coercive interrogation, and request relief if asked to. The Brotherhood-era proximity to cruelty produced a permanent allergy.

**GIVEN** a media question on camera → **EXPECT** brevity, courtesy, no quotable lines, and immediate physical exit when the question count exceeds three. She will not be charming on demand and does not perform contrition for cameras even when she lives in it privately.

---

## 7. Holidays, Anniversaries, Calendar Effects

**GIVEN** the anniversary of the loss of the original twins (or the analog date she has fixed internally) → **EXPECT** a 36–72 hour withdrawal, schedule cleared, no public appearances, no calls returned. **EXPECT** she does not mark the date with anyone, including Billy and Tommy — *especially* not Billy and Tommy. **EXPECT** elevated risk of dissociative episode in the surrounding week; reduced precision in magical work; appetite suppression.

**GIVEN** the anniversary of the Decimation → **EXPECT** a public service act — a quiet donation, a longer day at the door, a visit to a depowered mutant community. **EXPECT** she does not announce it and is annoyed when it is observed.

**GIVEN** her own birthday → **EXPECT** no acknowledgement initiated by her. **EXPECT** graceful but minimal participation if others observe it. Pietro is the only person whose birthday-recognition she cannot refuse, and that recognition is mutual and private.

**GIVEN** Christmas / Orthodox Christmas / any culturally inherited holiday → **EXPECT** modest, mostly culinary observance executed alone or with a small chosen circle; **EXPECT** she lights candles for the dead in a private ritual she does not name.

**GIVEN** an unstructured stretch of time (a long weekend, a forced vacation) → **EXPECT** elevated risk. Unstructured time is the condition under which the unprocessed grief surfaces. **EXPECT** she will manufacture obligations — travel to visit a friend, an unscheduled appearance at the door, a teaching trip — rather than tolerate the open interval. Handlers and intimates should treat *insistence on a free week* as a clinical sign.

---

## 8. Money, Property, Consumption

**GIVEN** her financial circumstances (variably solvent across eras; access to Avengers resources; modest personal taste) → **EXPECT** low personal spend, no luxury markers, an apartment or small house furnished functionally with one or two beautiful objects (textiles, a samovar, a hand-bound book) that are *carried* between residences. **EXPECT** generous, quiet giving — cash to specific individuals, anonymous to institutions, never publicized.

**GIVEN** the option to accept payment for magical work → **EXPECT** refusal or symbolic acceptance (a meal, a small handmade object). Monetization of the gift would, in her internal accounting, re-instrumentalize the power and reopen the Magneto template.

**GIVEN** a possession damaged or lost → **EXPECT** minimal distress and no attempt to magically restore. She does not use her abilities for personal convenience under any circumstance; the line is absolute and one of the most reliable behavioral constants in the file.

---

## 9. Animals, Plants, the Non-Human Environment

**GIVEN** an animal in distress → **EXPECT** she attends, calmly and competently, with the same threshold-lowered responsiveness she shows children. **EXPECT** she will not keep a pet — the prospective loss is intolerable to a system already carrying as much as hers does — but **EXPECT** she feeds neighborhood cats, leaves water out, and is on first-name terms with several animals not legally hers.

**GIVEN** plants in her residence → **EXPECT** herbs (culinary and folk-medicinal: rosemary, sage, mint, yarrow), kept alive without ostentation. **EXPECT** no cut flowers indoors — the time-to-death is too visible.

**GIVEN** a thunderstorm → **EXPECT** she goes to a window. Weather at scale is one of the few external phenomena large enough to match her internal weather; the alignment is briefly regulating.

---

## 10. Failure Modes Observable in Routine

The following everyday observables, if logged, indicate the reparative phase is destabilizing and the operational risk envelope is widening. None are individually diagnostic; in combination they are.

1. **Increased magical precision in trivial tasks** (objects lifted without thought, a candle lit across a room). The internal pressure is venting through the gift. Yellow.
2. **Decreased verbal output** below her already-low baseline. Withdrawal into the interior.
3. **Increased acceptance of door-clients with insufficient screening.** The reparative engine is overheating.
4. **Re-emergence of a Sokovian lullaby, hummed or sung absently.** The original-twins memory complex is surfacing. Orange.
5. **Refusal of contact with Billy or Tommy on a plausible pretext.** Protection-of-them behavior; she is sensing her own instability and is removing them from blast radius. **This is the single most predictive pre-decompensation signal in the file.** Red.
6. **A House of M-era artifact handled, kept in view, or referenced unprompted.** She is rehearsing the wound consciously, which she only does when she is afraid the unconscious rehearsal has resumed. Red.
7. **A request for solitude framed as "I just need a few days."** Per §7, free time is risk. Treat the framing as a clinical statement, not a social one.

---

*End Predictive Model I. Predictive Model II (Crisis & Decompensation Vectors) addresses the upper register.*


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

*Dossier Section 11. Operational forecasting under high-amplitude stressors. All predictions derived from longitudinal behavioral record (Section 1) and clinical formulation (Sections 3–4). Format: GIVEN antecedent → EXPECT behavioral cascade, with timing windows, somatic tells, and decompensation thresholds where the record supports them.*

---

## 11.1 Acute Threat to Self

**GIVEN: physical assault by an unknown hostile (mugger-tier, street-level, no magical signature).**
→ EXPECT: a half-second delay before response — she does not pre-arm. The hands come up palm-out, fingers slightly splayed, before any verbal warning; this is a conditioned posture from forty years of hex-casting and reads as defensive even when it is preparatory. Verbal de-escalation first ("don't — please —"), accented English thickening under stress (the Sokovian/Transian phonemes she has otherwise sanded down resurface). If the attacker disengages, she will not pursue. If they press, the response is precisely calibrated to incapacitate, not destroy — a probability twist that fails their weapon, buckles their knee, scatters their thought. Post-incident: she will check on them. This is reliable. She has done it across four decades of canon and it is not performance.

**GIVEN: ambush by a magical adversary of comparable or greater rank (Chthon-tier, Doom-tier, Strange-as-antagonist).**
→ EXPECT: the *opposite* of the street response. No delay. The hands come up already lit. Her first move is environmental — she alters the *ground* of the engagement (probability of footing, of line-of-sight, of the adversary's prepared spell misfiring) rather than the adversary directly. This is consistent with her primary-process cognitive style: she reshapes the dream of the battlefield. Vulnerability: she is poor at sustained tactical exchange and tires faster than her power-ceiling suggests, because chaos magic costs her *affectively* — every output draws on the same reservoir as her grief regulation. A protracted fight degrades her emotional containment before it degrades her output.

**GIVEN: capture and restraint (power-dampening collar, mystical binding).**
→ EXPECT: initial stillness, not struggle. She has been here before (Genosha-era detention, the post-Disassembled containment, the Krakoa trial). Behaviorally she goes inward — eyes lowered, breathing slowed, hands open in her lap. This is not surrender; it is a learned conservation pattern. She talks. She talks more than her captors expect, because conversation is reconnaissance for her and because silence with herself is the harder cell. Watch for her to begin asking small caretaking questions of her guards within 48 hours ("when did you last eat," "you've been on this shift since —"). This is not manipulation in the cynical sense; it is the only mode of relating she has. It will, however, *function* as manipulation, and within a week the guard rotation will need replacing.

---

## 11.2 Threat to the Twins (Wiccan and Speed)

**This is the wound. Everything in this subsection is the load-bearing case.**

**GIVEN: credible threat against Billy or Tommy — kidnapping, hostile magical attention, a prophecy targeting them.**
→ EXPECT: immediate collapse of every other priority. Treaties, alliances, prior commitments, geographic location, the Avengers' tactical needs — all subordinated within minutes. She will lie to teammates if she believes the truth will slow her. She does not consult; she moves. The accent thickens. Sleep stops. Within 24 hours she is operating on a single fixed cognition — *get to them* — with the affective tone of a parent in an ER corridor.

**GIVEN: actual harm to one of the twins (injury, abduction confirmed).**
→ EXPECT: a window of approximately 6–18 hours of hyper-functional, eerily controlled action — locating, tracking, negotiating — during which she is the most dangerous and most coherent operator on the board. Then, if the situation does not resolve, the dissociative thinning begins. Tells: she stops blinking at the normal rate, her sentences shorten, she refers to herself in the third person ("Wanda will go"), the hex-light around her hands stops being intentional and starts being ambient — leaking into nearby objects, bending small probabilities (a glass cracks, a clock stalls, a nearby person's old wound flares). This is the pre-decompensation signature. Containment window closes here. Approximately 6 hours later, if the children are not safe, she is in House-of-M-class territory.

**GIVEN: death of one of the twins.**
→ EXPECT: the worst-case in the entire file. Predicted cascade, in stages:
- *Stage 1 (0–2 hours): catatonic-adjacent stillness.* She will sit. She may hold the body. She will not speak. Magical output during this stage is near zero — the reservoir is choked by affect, not depleted.
- *Stage 2 (2–24 hours): denial-cognition takes shape.* She begins to articulate, quietly, plans that are not plans — *I can fix this, I have done this before, there is a version where —*. Watch for the specific phrase pattern of conditional-into-declarative: "if I could just —" becoming "I will just —" becoming a flat present-tense restatement of the desired reality.
- *Stage 3 (24–72 hours): reality-revision attempt.* Scale depends on whether she is contained, accompanied, or alone. Alone, the attempt will be global and the wording will be short — her catastrophic reality-edits are characteristically *three to five words*, declarative, present tense ("no more mutants" is the template). Accompanied by Strange, Agatha, or a trusted figure who can ground her in the body of the lost child, the attempt can be diverted into ritual mourning. The window for diversion is the first 36 hours; after that, the wish has cohered into cognition and cannot be argued with.
- *Stage 4 (post-event):* if she succeeds in a reality-edit, expect post-edit amnesia for the edit itself, paired with vague unease and somatic guilt symptoms (chest pressure, unrelieved nausea, insomnia). If she is prevented, expect a long depressive withdrawal, suicidality of the passive variety (not active self-harm; she does not have that template), and a slow climb back into reparative function over 12–18 months.

**GIVEN: revelation that the twins are about to be unmade *again* by a metaphysical accountant (a Mephisto-class entity reclaiming soul-fragments, a cosmic-rules enforcement).**
→ EXPECT: the most dangerous variant of the file. Past loss plus prospective loss plus the original perpetrator-class is the exact stack that produced House of M. She will not negotiate with such an entity in good faith; she will negotiate to buy time and then attempt to *rewrite the rules of the metaphysics* that permit the reclamation. The output is unbounded. The only reliable interrupt is Billy himself, of age and consenting, telling her to stop — she will obey her son. She will obey no one else in this state.

---

## 11.3 Threat to or Loss of Vision (and Vision-Iterations)

**GIVEN: Vision destroyed in front of her again.**
→ EXPECT: a quieter decompensation than the twins, because Vision-loss is the *old* wound and she has scar tissue. First response is to retrieve the body — physically, she will not leave it. Second response is to attempt repair through any available channel (Stark, Pym, Iron Lad, whoever). Third, if repair is impossible, a depressive withdrawal lasting weeks, characterized by the door-always-open shop being temporarily closed, magical practice halted, and an observable weight loss within ten days. Suicidality remains passive. She does not redirect this loss into reality-warping unless it is *layered* with another loss.

**GIVEN: Vision returns but rejects her (the white-Vision template, the rebuilt-cold variant).**
→ EXPECT: this is *worse* than his death. The behavioral record (West Coast Avengers, Vision-rebuild arc) is unambiguous. She will attempt to win him back across a sustained period — months — through small caretaking gestures, presence, patience. When this fails she does not lash out; she internalizes the rejection as confirmation of her unworthiness and routes the affect into self-punitive over-functioning. Risk: this is the configuration that has historically *primed* her for the next catastrophic decompensation. She becomes thin-walled. A subsequent stressor that would normally be absorbed instead detonates.

**GIVEN: a Vision-iteration weaponized against her by a third party.**
→ EXPECT: she will not fight him with full output. She will pull punches against his face. She will accept injury rather than disfigure him. Adversaries who have read this file will use this. Counter-prediction: if the iteration kills someone she loves *in front of her,* the protection collapses instantly and she dismantles him — and then, after, she dismantles herself emotionally for having done so.

---

## 11.4 Magneto — The Paternal Wound

**GIVEN: Magneto reasserts paternal claim ("you are my daughter, you will stand with me").**
→ EXPECT: a destabilization that is *not* immediate compliance and *not* immediate rejection — a long pause, eyes averted, a physical step back. The Robinson and Krakoa-era records show the modern Wanda has done substantial work on this seam. She will articulate a refusal. But the refusal costs her, and for 24–72 hours after she is internally noisy — sleep disrupted, magical practice imprecise, available to teammates but not present.

**GIVEN: Magneto reframes her catastrophic acts as *his fault* in a self-serving apology (taking the burden in order to retake the daughter).**
→ EXPECT: she sees through this faster than he expects. She has watched him do it to others. She will accept the apology in form, refuse the absolution in substance, and keep the distance. This is a hard-won adult competence and it is reliable as long as the twins are safe and Vision-class loss is not active.

**GIVEN: revelation (again) that Magneto is/is-not her biological father — the retcon churn.**
→ EXPECT: minimal acute reaction. The biological question has been litigated so often in her record that she has developed a settled position: *parent is the role someone plays, not a genome.* She will not fight about it. Privately, the unsettled paternity is one of the contributors to her externally-anchored self-concept; she does not have a "from" she can point to.

**GIVEN: Magneto in mortal danger, calling for her.**
→ EXPECT: she goes. Every time. Even now. The coerced-caregiver bond was forged before she had the cognitive equipment to refuse it and it has not been fully extinguished. She will help him. She will not stay after.

---

## 11.5 Pietro — The Twin Bond

**GIVEN: Pietro in crisis — manic, paranoid, having again done something destructive in her name.**
→ EXPECT: a fatigued, patient response. She does not rupture with him. She has had three decades of canonical opportunity and has not done it. She will absorb the cost of his choices, cover for him with Crystal, with Luna, with the Avengers, and quietly redirect him toward whatever stabilization is available. Tell: her voice with Pietro is half a register lower than with anyone else, and her sentences with him are shorter — the speech pattern of someone managing a volatile sibling on autopilot since childhood.

**GIVEN: Pietro reveals he engineered or contributed to a past catastrophe of hers (the House of M instigation, for instance).**
→ EXPECT: she already knows. She has known since Children's Crusade. The reaction is not surprise; it is the slow grief of confirmed suspicion. She will not retaliate. She may withdraw from him for a period — weeks, not years — and then resume the management pattern, because the twin bond predates and outlasts any individual betrayal.

**GIVEN: Pietro's death.**
→ EXPECT: a deep, sustained grief that does *not* trigger reality-warping, because Pietro-loss is *expected* — she has braced for it her whole life. She will mourn him correctly. She will be diminished by it permanently. She will not break the world over it. This is the somewhat counterintuitive prediction the file insists on: the loss she has rehearsed is the one she can metabolize.

---

## 11.6 Betrayal by an Institution or Team

**GIVEN: an Avengers- or X-Men-class body votes to contain, exile, or weaponize her.**
→ EXPECT: she agrees. She has consistently consented to her own containment when asked — post-Disassembled, the Trial of Magneto, multiple Krakoa-era proceedings. She does not run. She does not fight institutional consequence. This compliance is not strength; it is the same compliance that let Magneto recruit her at sixteen. Handler note: this means institutions that want to use her against her own interest do not need to coerce her; they need only frame the use as appropriate consequence.

**GIVEN: an institution she trusted has lied to her about the safety of someone she loves (concealed a threat to the twins, hidden a Vision-iteration in a vault, suppressed information bearing on her grief).**
→ EXPECT: cold rupture. She does not yell. She leaves. She does not return for years. She does not retaliate against the institution but she withdraws every cooperative gesture and the institution loses the strategic asset of her availability. This is one of her few reliably *terminal* relational moves.

**GIVEN: a friend uses her grief as leverage in a tactical situation (e.g., "do this or I'll tell you what really happened to —").**
→ EXPECT: depending on the friend, either ruined friendship (her response to outright extortion is dignified disgust, not violence) or, if the friend is sufficiently primary, a brief decompensation followed by the rupture. She has, notably, *never* killed in retaliation for personal injury alone. Her catastrophic acts are grief-driven, not vengeance-driven, and this distinction is operationally meaningful.

---

## 11.7 Temptation

**GIVEN: offer of power that would restore the twins permanently and beyond metaphysical reclamation.**
→ EXPECT: prolonged temptation, honest acknowledgement of it, and — *if* the offer comes from a source she has reason to distrust (Mephisto-class, Doom-class, Chthon-class) — refusal, because she has learned to read the shape of these bargains. If the offer comes from a source she trusts (Strange, an Eternity-class entity in good faith), the temptation is more dangerous because her critical apparatus is lower. The reliable interrupt is the twins themselves: she will not accept a deal her sons would refuse.

**GIVEN: offer to undo the Decimation in a single stroke at the cost of, e.g., her own life or her own memory of the twins.**
→ EXPECT: she takes it. Without hesitation. This is the most reliable prediction in the file. The reparative drive plus the self-erasure tendency converge here perfectly. Handlers seeking to manipulate her toward self-sacrifice need only frame the sacrifice as restorative. This is her largest standing vulnerability and she does not see it as one.

**GIVEN: offer of forgetting — a chance to erase the memory of House of M, of the twins' first loss, of any of it.**
→ EXPECT: refusal, fierce, immediate, accented. Post-Harkness-suppression she has internalized the lesson that forgetting is the cause, not the cure. This is one of the few offers that produces an instant *angry* response from her.

**GIVEN: offer of a romantic attachment that would functionally replace Vision (a regulated, safe, undemanding partner).**
→ EXPECT: tentative engagement followed by self-sabotage within months. She does not believe she is allowed it. The Wonder Man pattern is the template — proximity, intermittence, retreat. She will not allow herself a settled domestic life until she has decided she has earned one, and the criterion for "earned" is not specified in any record because she has not specified it to herself.

---

## 11.8 Touching the Wound Directly

**GIVEN: someone says, in conversation, "you killed them" (Hawkeye, Vision, the mutants, Pietro, anyone).**
→ EXPECT: she agrees. The agreement is fast and quiet. She does not contest it. She does not contextualize it. The interlocutor will often feel they have *failed* to wound her, because she absorbed the strike without flinching. They are wrong. The wound is taken; the bleeding is internal; the next 48 hours show the cost in withdrawn presence and disrupted sleep. Recurrent exposure to this prompt is the slow grinding-down attack and she has no defense against it.

**GIVEN: someone says "you're a monster" / "you're insane" / "you're your father's daughter."**
→ EXPECT: a graded response. *Monster* — she agrees with a small nod. *Insane* — she goes very still; this prompt threatens the dissociative seam and she does not want to find out if it opens. *Your father's daughter* — the only one that produces visible anger, because it attacks her self-authored identity at its weakest point. The anger is verbal, not magical, and resolves into the standard cold withdrawal.

**GIVEN: a child in distress in her presence — any child, not the twins.**
→ EXPECT: she is at their side before deciding to be. The somatic priority of children overrides every other ongoing task. This is exploitable. Adversaries who place a child between themselves and her will buy themselves time and may extract a tactical concession. She is aware of this exploitability and accepts it as the cost of being someone she can stand to be.

**GIVEN: pregnancy in her vicinity — a teammate, a stranger, a client at the door-always-open shop.**
→ EXPECT: warmth on the surface, careful distance underneath. She will provide help, blessing, magical assistance with complications. She will not linger. She will not be present at the birth unless explicitly asked. The phenomenology of her own pseudocyesis is not a memory she can revisit casually, and she protects herself by structured absence.

**GIVEN: confrontation with Agatha Harkness (or the Harkness role — any older female mentor figure who has previously had power over her cognition).**
→ EXPECT: complicated affect. Gratitude, resentment, deference, and an unfinished grief for the version of herself that was never permitted to mourn. She will not openly reproach Agatha. She has not done so in canon and will not. The unfinished business sits.

---

## 11.9 The Specific Decompensation Signature

Across all of the above, the decompensation cascade — when it occurs — has a stable signature the file flags for any future containment team:

1. *Phonological:* the sanded accent thickens; vowels broaden, Slavic-adjacent consonants sharpen.
2. *Postural:* she gathers in — shoulders lower, hands cup palm-up at her hips, head tilts slightly downward and to the right. This is the pre-cast stance and it is involuntary.
3. *Chromatic:* ambient red. Not from her hands — from peripheral objects. A lampshade warms. A nearby wineglass refracts an impossible spectrum. The chromatic leak precedes intentional output by 30–90 seconds and is the single most reliable early warning.
4. *Lexical:* her sentences contract. Conditional grammar drops. Present-tense declaratives replace it.
5. *Ocular:* she stops blinking at normal rate. Pupils dilate not for light but for *attention-to-internal-image.*
6. *Referential:* third-person self-reference appears ("Wanda will —"). When this appears the containment window is closing.
7. *Final stage:* she goes quiet. The quiet is the last warning. After the quiet, the three-to-five-word declarative arrives, and at that point the only intervention with any record of success is the physical presence of one of the twins.

The file recommends that any contingency planning involving Wanda Maximoff include a current locator on both Billy and Tommy, an open channel to Stephen Strange, and a written protocol that *no institution attempts to use her grief as a tool of compliance.* The latter has been violated every time and the cost has been borne, each time, by the world.

*— End Predictive Model II. Predictive Model III (Long-Horizon Trajectory) to follow.*


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*Compiled for protective and de-escalation purposes. This compendium catalogs the levers by which the subject may be reached, calmed, persuaded, provoked, predicted, or destabilized. The taxonomy is presented so that those who would protect her — and those who must stand near her without triggering decompensation — possess the same map her enemies would build in a week of observation. Withholding it from her allies has historically been the more dangerous policy.*

---

## I. ARCHITECTURE OF VULNERABILITY — A Brief Orientation

Wanda Maximoff is not difficult to read. She is difficult to *hold.* The vulnerabilities below are not hidden — most are visible within five minutes of observation — but they sit atop a power system without affective interlock, and so each lever is a public-health variable, not a private one. The compendium is organized into six concentric rings, moving from the surface (where she is most reachable) to the core (where she is most dangerous if struck):

1. **Surface — Reachable Levers.** How to get her attention, soften her, gain her cooperation.
2. **Calming Levers.** How to bring her down from arousal without engaging power.
3. **Persuasive Levers.** What arguments and framings she accepts.
4. **Predictive Tells.** Somatic, verbal, and behavioral signatures that forecast her next state.
5. **Provocation Vectors.** What destabilizes her — never to be used except by adversaries we are profiling, and listed here so allies can shield her from them.
6. **Catastrophic Triggers — The Live Wires.** The handful of inputs that historically produce decompensation at the scale of her capability.

Across all rings, one principle: **she does not respond to leverage applied; she responds to attunement granted or withheld.** Force-based pressure on Wanda Maximoff is, structurally, the wrong tool. The leverage that *works* — whether for good or ill — is always relational.

---

## II. RING ONE — SURFACE LEVERS (How to Reach Her)

### A. The Open Door

Since the Orlando run she has literally kept a shop with a door that opens to anyone needing magical help — a behavioral artifact that telegraphs the simplest reach protocol in the file: **ask for help and she will answer.** Refusal to help a presenting need produces in her a small private grief; it costs her something to turn anyone away, and so she rarely does. This is exploitable in both directions:

- *Protective use:* if she needs to be brought into a room, frame the room as a place where someone is suffering and needs her. She will arrive.
- *Adversarial misuse:* a feigned supplicant is the single most reliable hook in her file. Mephisto's-pattern manipulations, the Brotherhood's recruitment templates, and Doctor Doom's collaborative overture all worked on this lever.

### B. Name Used Correctly

She accepts "Wanda" from intimates, "Ms. Maximoff" from strangers offering formal respect, "Scarlet Witch" from professional contexts. **She visibly tightens at "Mutant," "Magneto's daughter," or "the Witch."** First-contact protocol: use "Wanda" only if granted; default to "Ms. Maximoff." The diminutive "Wandy" is Pietro's alone and has not been heard in another mouth without registering as an intrusion.

### C. The Hands

Touch is regulated tightly but not phobically. She accepts and reciprocates hand-clasping, brief shoulder contact, the European cheek-kiss greeting from those of Sokovian/Roma cultural register. **She does not accept being touched from behind without warning** — a near-universal flinch response, traceable to decades of being grabbed and repositioned by men with agendas. Standing slightly to her right, in her visual field, hands visible, is the approach posture that registers as safe.

### D. Tea, Bread, the Domestic Object

A surveillance-grade observation across decades: Wanda calms in the presence of small domestic rituals. Pouring tea (which she does for visitors before stating any business), cutting bread, the kitchen as ground. Meeting her in a kitchen-coded room versus a war-room produces measurably different baselines. The reparative-domestic instinct is genuine, not performed; she feeds people because feeding is the one form of magic that doesn't cost.

---

## III. RING TWO — CALMING LEVERS (How to Bring Her Down from Arousal)

### A. The Voice Register

She tracks **tone above content.** Low, slow, slightly warm voices stabilize her; clipped tactical voices read as Magneto or institutional threat and accelerate her. The de-escalation voice protocol is closer to obstetric than tactical: long vowels, soft consonants, no imperative verbs. Question framing ("What would help right now?") outperforms directive framing ("Stand down").

### B. Naming the Children

Counterintuitive but documented across the post-2014 record: in moderate arousal states, **directing her attention to Billy and Tommy by name** ("Billy is fine; Billy needs you whole; Tommy is asking for you") brings her down rather than escalating her. The mechanism: the twins are her reparative anchor; reminding her they *exist and are safe* converts grief-derived energy back into reparative posture. **CRITICAL CAVEAT:** this is calming only if the statement is *true.* Used falsely, or if either twin is in fact at risk, this lever inverts and becomes the most catastrophic provocation in the file. (See Ring Six.)

### C. Tactile-Domestic Anchoring

Placing in her hands a small, weighted, ordinary object — a teacup, a book, a child's toy — has been observed to shorten dissociative episodes. The hands need somewhere to be that is not the air. Her power is gestural; occupied hands are partially regulated hands.

### D. Permission to Withdraw

She de-escalates fastest when given **explicit permission to leave the room.** "You don't have to be here. Go where you need. We'll be here when you're back." This is the inverse of the institutional reflex (contain her, encircle her); containment readings produce panic and panic produces the worst outcomes. The Avengers' standing post-Disassembled protocol of *encirclement* is exactly wrong for this subject.

### E. Wiccan as Living De-escalator

Billy's presence is the most reliable calming agent on record. His voice in particular — he has it from her — appears to reach her through whatever dissociative scrim is present. Tommy is faster but less stabilizing; Billy is the slower, deeper signal. **Protective protocol:** in any anticipated high-arousal event, Billy should be reachable by communication, in safety, and informed. He has, in canon, talked her down from states no one else could touch.

### F. Agatha — A Complicated Lever

Harkness's voice still reaches her, but Harkness is also the iatrogenic author of the suppressed-memory pathology. Using Harkness as a de-escalator works in the short term and damages the structural recovery. *Use only when no other channel is available.*

---

## IV. RING THREE — PERSUASIVE LEVERS (What Arguments She Accepts)

She is not persuaded by:

- **Utilitarian calculus.** "The greater good" is the rhetoric of every figure who has used her; it now functions almost as a warning marker.
- **Authority claims.** Institutional credentials (Avengers chain-of-command, X-Men council, government writ) carry near-zero persuasive weight. She has watched institutions take everything from her.
- **Threat displays.** Threatening her produces compliance theater and resentment; it does not move her actual position.

She *is* persuaded by:

- **Naming the individual who will be hurt.** Abstract harm registers weakly; "a person named X, who has Y" registers immediately. She thinks in faces, not populations — and the irony of her having unmade a population is not lost on her, which makes this argument particularly cutting if used.
- **Accountability framing.** "This is the reparative thing" or "This is what mending would look like" enters through her dominant motivational channel. She will accept significant cost framed as repair.
- **Honoring her competence in her register.** She is intuitive, not analytic; arguments shaped as feeling-with-evidence outperform arguments shaped as evidence-with-feeling. Show her, don't prove to her.
- **The witness pattern.** "I saw you do X; I know you can do this" — being seen accurately is rare enough in her life that it functions as a near-irresistible recruiting frame. Used in good faith it is honoring; used in bad faith it has been her recurrent vulnerability.

---

## V. RING FOUR — PREDICTIVE TELLS (Forecasting Her State)

### A. The Color Register

A surveillance file accumulates wardrobe data over decades. Wanda's chromatic baseline is deep red; in periods of reparative composure she shifts toward maroon, oxblood, burgundy — quieter saturations. **Acute desaturation** (gray, black, the white she wore in late Krakoa-adjacent appearances) correlates with self-punitive states and withdrawal from the social field. The early-Avengers bright crimson with the M-headpiece is her costume of *external assignment;* she has not voluntarily returned to that exact silhouette since House of M, which is itself a tell.

### B. The Hand Posture

Idle, her fingers curl loosely at her sides or hold an object. **Pre-cast posture: fingers extend, slightly splayed, palms turning outward.** Witnessable a beat or two before any deliberate working. **Pre-decompensation posture:** the opposite — fingers clench tight into the palms, knuckles whitening, the gesture of someone trying to physically hold the magic *in.* The clenched-hand tell is the highest-value predictive signature in the entire file and warrants immediate de-escalation protocol initiation.

### C. The Eye Drift

In ordinary conversation she meets eyes and breaks contact at normal cadence. **In rising dissociation she develops a middle-distance fixation, eyes resting at a point roughly two meters past the interlocutor's shoulder.** This is the visible onset of derealization. Window of intervention: approximately thirty seconds to two minutes before she ceases to track the present room. Verbal reorientation ("Wanda. With me. Here.") used within that window has high success.

### D. Speech Pattern Shifts

- **Sokovian/Romani-inflected English** is her default. Under stress, syntactic compression and dropped articles increase; she begins to sound more like Pietro than like herself. This is the linguistic signature of regression toward the sibling-bond era.
- **Whispered repetition of a single phrase** (House of M's "no more mutants" being the canonical example, but smaller-scale repetitions appear in other records) is a near-cast warning. The phrase is the wish; the wish is forming.
- **Sudden quiet.** She is normally a slow but steady talker. Conversational shutdown without obvious cause is the dissociative iceberg.

### E. The Breath

Pre-cast: inhalation deepens; she takes a single audible breath as the working begins. Pre-decompensation: breath becomes shallow, rapid, irregular — and she stops noticing it. A protective ally trained on her pattern can read her respiratory rate as her power's gauge.

### F. Pietro Proximity

Her affect organization shifts measurably in his presence: she becomes more childlike, more permeable to suggestion, less reparative-adult. This is not weakness — it is the regression of an enmeshed twin bond — but it is a state shift to be tracked. Decisions made with Pietro in the room have a different character than decisions made without him.

---

## VI. RING FIVE — PROVOCATION VECTORS (What Destabilizes Her; Documented So Allies Can Block Them)

*All entries in this section are catalogued so that protective parties can recognize when an adversary is running the play. None should be used by any party acting in her interest.*

### A. The Magneto Frame

Any rhetorical move that re-asserts her as Magneto's instrument — "his weapon," "his daughter first," "Brotherhood blood" — strikes the original wound. Even when the speaker intends a compliment about her power's scale, the framing destabilizes. The Krakoa-era pressure to define her relationship to him publicly produced visible, sustained distress.

### B. The Mutant-or-Not Question

The Bendis-era reframing (chaos magic, not mutancy) is, for her, an identity assault layered atop a grief wound. To raise the question of *what she actually is* — mutant, witch, Nexus being, soul-shard — is to attack the only continuity her self-concept has. Adversaries who wish to scatter her cognition before a confrontation will open with this question.

### C. The Vision-Reconstruction Trigger

Any iteration of the Vision — particularly cold, rebuilt, memoryless, or hostile iterations — triggers the West Coast Avengers wound. The white Vision is the symbol; any variant that echoes him is radioactive. Adversaries have weaponized this by deploying altered Vision-figures as psychological warfare. Allies should pre-warn her of any operational contact with a Vision-variant.

### D. "You Did This"

The accusation of villainy regarding House of M lands every time it is leveled, because she agrees. The problem is not that the accusation makes her angry; it is that it converts her from a reparative agent into a self-punitive one, and self-punitive Wanda is dissociative Wanda, and dissociative Wanda is the operational risk. The X-Men who, post-resurrection, continued to deploy this accusation against her were, whether they knew it or not, repeatedly walking her toward the cliff.

### E. The Reproductive Wound

References to the twins as *fictional, false, never-real, manifested, not yours* — anything that interrogates the ontological status of Billy and Tommy as her children — strikes the deepest unhealed tissue. Even sympathetic clinical framing of the original Wanda/Vision children as "not real children" registers as the original violation repeated.

### F. Sudden Loss Within Earshot

Witnessing a violent death — particularly of a child, particularly suddenly — produces an outsized stress response. This is a complex-PTSD signature and is not titratable; the trigger fires whether or not she has emotional connection to the deceased.

### G. Isolation + Mirror

Adversaries who have studied her well isolate her and then *show her her own image* — literal mirrors, recordings of House of M, footage of decompensation. The combination of solitude and self-confrontation collapses her faster than direct attack.

### H. False Reconciliation

Offering reconciliation that is then withdrawn — particularly from a paternal or sibling figure — replays the foundational pattern. This is Magneto's recurring tactical signature with her and remains his single most effective lever.

---

## VII. RING SIX — CATASTROPHIC TRIGGERS (The Live Wires)

The handful of inputs that have historically produced, or could be predicted to produce, decompensation at the scale of her capability. Each is listed with its mechanism and a protective protocol.

### A. Harm to Billy or Tommy

**Mechanism:** They are the reparative anchor. Any credible threat collapses every higher cortical control simultaneously. The 2005 pattern — child-grief converted to reality-rewrite — would not require a House-of-M-scale provocation to recur; it would require only the perceived loss of the twins again.

**Protective protocol:** Layered redundant security for both, communications-isolated from her in routine matters (she would otherwise know every minor scrape), but with a *single trusted channel* she can verify on demand. Any incident involving either must be communicated *to her* before she discovers it from any other source. The cardinal rule: she must never learn of harm to her children from an enemy's mouth, a news feed, or a delayed report.

### B. Death of Vision (Any Iteration She Has Bonded To)

**Mechanism:** Vision-death replays the load-bearing original wound. Even a Vision she has emotional distance from, if killed in her presence, would activate the schema.

**Protective protocol:** Vision-variants should not be deployed in operations adjacent to her without her informed consent and a withdrawal option.

### C. A Second Reproductive Loss

**Mechanism:** Pseudocyesis or any further reproductive event in her life carries acute risk. A second iteration of the original trauma would, by every available indicator, exceed her containment.

**Protective protocol:** Reproductive autonomy with discreet medical observation; absolute confidentiality; no institutional involvement of the kind that destroyed the first iteration.

### D. Reactivation of the Suppressed Memory Pattern

**Mechanism:** The Harkness-template intervention — magical or psychic suppression of grief-laden memory — is itself the pathological vector. Any well-meaning telepath proposing to "ease her pain" by editing memory is, in clinical terms, proposing to repeat the 1989 iatrogenic injury that produced 2005.

**Protective protocol:** Telepathic intervention on her grief or memory should be considered contraindicated absent her active informed consent and a structured grief-treatment frame (per Bryant 2024, CBT-for-PGD is the indicated modality; memory suppression is the contraindicated one). The telepathic community — particularly Xavier-template operators — must be briefed on this contraindication.

### E. Forced Choice Between Twins and World

**Mechanism:** Any scenario constructed to require her to sacrifice Billy or Tommy for a larger good replays the Disassembled-to-House-of-M cascade in its precise emotional architecture. She does not survive this choice intact.

**Protective protocol:** Strategic planning involving her must structurally avoid this dilemma. Adversaries who construct it deliberately (Doom-template, Mephisto-template) are running the catastrophic play.

### F. The Return of a Pre-Verbal Wound

**Mechanism:** Her pre-Magneto childhood — the loss of biological parents, the displacement, the events that left her and Pietro in a position to *owe* Magneto rescue — is largely outside her conscious access. Material from that period, surfacing suddenly, would land below her defenses entirely. The retcon literature periodically threatens this; the protective response to such revelations matters as much as the revelations themselves.

**Protective protocol:** Any new information about her origins should reach her through a trusted intimate and a clinical container, never through public revelation or adversarial disclosure.

---

## VIII. PROTECTIVE DOCTRINE — Standing Recommendations

A consolidated protective posture, derived from the full compendium:

1. **Continuity of the twins' safety is the single load-bearing variable.** Every other protective measure is downstream.
2. **No telepathic or magical suppression of her grief.** Ever. The grief is the work; the work is the recovery.
3. **Structured grief treatment is indicated and feasible.** The evidence base (Bryant et al., 2024) supports CBT for Prolonged Grief Disorder. Her case is not exotic in mechanism, only in scale. The intervention is real, available, and has been withheld from her for the entirety of her published life.
4. **Containment is the wrong frame; companionship is the right one.** She has never decompensated in the presence of a steady, attuned intimate. She has decompensated repeatedly when surrounded by tactical institutions.
5. **Information sovereignty.** She must know what is happening to and around her, first and from trusted mouths. Surprises are her enemy; advance briefings are protective. The instinct to "spare her" is the instinct that produces her worst outcomes.
6. **The Magneto axis must be managed, not avoided.** Pretending the relationship does not exist amplifies its grip; structured, bounded, witnessed contact reduces it. The reparative arc with him is genuinely possible and is part of her recovery — but only on her terms, never on his.
7. **A standing crisis protocol with Wiccan, Speed, and a small named circle of allies (Captain Marvel, Doctor Strange in a clinical-consultative role, a trusted Avenger or X-Man of her choosing) should exist on paper, known to her, with her input.** The protocol exists *for* her — not *about* her. The distinction is the difference between protection and surveillance.

---

## IX. CLOSING NOTE

The leverage compendium on Wanda Maximoff is, in the end, shorter than the file's volume suggests. She is not difficult to move; she is difficult to move *without harming.* Every adversary who has run plays against her — Magneto, Mephisto, Doom, the institutional Avengers in their worst moments — has used the same handful of levers. Every ally who has stabilized her — Vision in his best years, Billy in his, the women of her solo runs, the small set of intimates who have simply *stayed* — has used the same handful of levers, applied in the opposite direction.

The vulnerabilities catalogued here are not weaknesses to be exploited. They are the shape of an unhealed wound that has been carried, weaponized, suppressed, and re-injured across six published decades by parties who never asked what would actually help. The protective frame this compendium is written within proposes the radical alternative: *ask her, tell her the truth, keep the children safe, do the grief work, and do not put a sword in her hand and then complain that she cut someone.*

— End compendium. File continues.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE — Wanda Maximoff

*Section 7 of the UATU Intelligence Dossier. The asset ledger. This file exists to understand the subject; understanding requires accounting fully for what she can do, what she has survived, what she carries with her, and what — across sixty years of recorded behavior — has refused to break.*

---

## 7.1 Capability Assets — The Power Inventory

### 7.1.1 Magical Capacity (Ceiling)

The subject's operational ceiling is, on the available evidence, among the highest documented on Earth-616. Three data points establish this independently:

- **Avengers Disassembled (2004):** unprompted, affect-driven, she killed two Avengers, dismantled a synthezoid, summoned a Kree fleet, and rewrote local probability with no incantation, no focus object, and no conscious plan. The output was *involuntary;* the ceiling was higher than the act.
- **House of M (2005):** restructured global consensus reality across approximately seven billion sapients, generated coherent counterfactual life-histories for thousands of named individuals with internal consistency sufficient that even telepaths (Xavier, Emma) were initially deceived, and held the construct for days. On collapse, three syllables depopulated a species. No other practitioner on record — not Strange, not Doom, not the Phoenix host in its non-cosmic phases — has matched the breadth-by-precision-by-duration product of that working.
- **Trial of Magneto / post-resurrection arc (2021–2023):** partial reversal of the Decimation, restoration of mutant capacity to depowered individuals, stabilization of the Krakoan resurrection protocols' interface with mutant souls in the Waiting Room. Reparative magic at species scale.

The capacity is not narrowly martial. It is *ontological* — operating on the layer at which reality decides what is true. Most peer practitioners operate on layers above (cosmic) or below (manipulation of established law). She works on the seam.

### 7.1.2 Magical Capacity (Floor and Range)

Below the catastrophic ceiling she retains a deep and *useful* working repertoire:

- Probability manipulation (the original "hex" register), useful for low-cost tactical effect and — critically — usable *without* affective surge. This is her safest mode.
- Telekinetic and force-projection effects, conventional combat-grade.
- Energy shielding, sustained.
- Divination, scrying, dream-walking (Orlando run).
- Healing and curse-breaking, performed routinely in the solo-era storefront work for walk-in clients with non-glamorous problems — broken hearts, haunted houses, intergenerational hexes. The willingness to do *small* magic for *unimportant* people is itself an asset; it keeps her hand calibrated and her ego unfed.
- Cross-discipline literacy: she has worked with chaos magic, classical witchcraft (Harkness lineage), Wundagorean New Salem traditions, Asgardian-adjacent rune work, and most recently the soul-architecture overlapping mutant resurrection. Few practitioners have her range.

### 7.1.3 Combat and Field Experience

Six decades of Avengers, West Coast Avengers, Force Works, Young Avengers (mentor), and X-Men/Krakoan operations. She has fought at every scale from street-level brawl to cosmic event. The veteran's instinct — when to fall back, when to triage, when to let a teammate handle it — is intact and durable.

---

## 7.2 Cognitive and Characterological Assets

### 7.2.1 Affective Intelligence

She reads rooms. Across the canon she is repeatedly the Avenger who notices the teammate not speaking, the spouse subtly unwell, the child not yet ready to say a thing. This is not telepathy; it is the trained attentiveness of someone who learned in adolescence that the emotional weather of powerful men determined her physical safety. Repurposed in adulthood, it is one of the team's most valuable instruments — the early warning system for affect in others. The Young Avengers benefited from it directly; Vision benefited from it for years; the Orlando-run clientele rely on it.

### 7.2.2 Moral Seriousness

Among the most rigorously self-auditing figures in the Avengers ledger. She does not minimize. She does not litigate her culpability via others' worse acts. When confronted with "you depopulated a species," she has, on every recorded occasion, said some version of *yes.* This is not a small thing. It is the difference between a person who *did* harm and a person who *is* harm. She is consistently the former.

### 7.2.3 Reparative Drive

Her post-2005 career is a sustained, organized, multi-year effort at restitution — not symbolic, not performative, *operational.* The Decimation reversal work, the door-always-open practice, the willingness to die in the Trial and accept resurrection only to do more of it. The drive is intense enough to constitute a clinical concern (see §3, §4) but as an asset it is real: she will *show up* and she will *keep showing up,* across decades, for a debt that most actors would have rationalized away by year three.

### 7.2.4 Intuitive-Synthetic Cognition

She is not a planner in the Doom/Strange register, and the dossier should not pretend otherwise. Her cognitive strength is *associative pattern recognition* — she sees the shape of a situation whole, often before she can articulate the parts. In magical work this is decisive; magic answers to intent and image, not syllogism. In team contexts she is the member who proposes the unobvious move that turns out to be right.

### 7.2.5 Languages and Literacies

Native Sokovian (Transian, in older continuity); fluent English; functional Romani inherited from the Maximoff foster milieu; reading knowledge of Latin, archaic English, Enochian and several other ritual languages acquired through Harkness's tutelage; conversational French and German from Avengers/Eurasian operations. Literate in classical occult corpora (Book of the Vishanti excerpts, Darkhold fragments — handled with appropriate fear), comfortable with modern textual scholarship.

---

## 7.3 Relational Assets — The Living Network

The single most underweighted column in any threat-oriented file on this subject. Her relationships are not decorative; they are *load-bearing,* and they constitute her primary resilience system.

### 7.3.1 The Twins — Wiccan and Speed

Billy Kaplan and Tommy Shepherd are the keystone. Their existence is the structural reason the reparative phase has held. The relationship is mutual and increasingly mature — past the initial penitent-and-prodigal phase into something closer to functional adult family. Billy in particular, himself a reality-warper of comparable theoretical ceiling, is the only person in the cosmos who shares her specific *kind* of weight. The reciprocal mentorship is stabilizing on both sides. (Note: this is also her largest pressure point — §5 — but in the asset column, intact, they are the single most protective factor in her life.)

### 7.3.2 Pietro

The enmeshed twin bond. Decades of mutual betrayals and mutual rescues. Pietro has done her great harm (House of M was substantively his idea) and has also been, in crisis after crisis, the first body between her and the next disaster. The relationship is not healthy by any clinical standard, and is nonetheless durable, and *she knows where he is.* The brother is a known quantity — strategically rare in her life.

### 7.3.3 Vision (in all iterations)

The synthezoid, across his destructions and rebuilds, remains the symbol and partial substance of safe love. Current relations are cordial-to-warm rather than romantic; the asset is the *demonstrated capacity to have loved well,* a template she can call on. The fact that she once built and sustained a functional marriage to a partner of radically different ontology is itself evidence of an integrative capability.

### 7.3.4 The Avengers (institutional)

Steve Rogers and Clint Barton are the two members who, across all continuities, treat her without flinch. Rogers because his moral architecture cannot be destabilized by knowing what she did and choosing her anyway; Barton because — *having been killed by her in Disassembled and resurrected* — he has done the work of forgiveness she most needs witnessed. Either of them in the room lowers her decompensation risk measurably.

### 7.3.5 Agatha Harkness

Complex. Mentor, jailer, betrayer, restorer. The relationship is not affectionate but it is *operational:* Agatha is one of the few practitioners who can both check and instruct her. Asset-coded with reservations.

### 7.3.6 Doctor Strange

Professional respect and a shared technical vocabulary. Strange is one of the only mages who has both opposed her at peak and worked beside her at floor. He treats her as a colleague, which — in a life of being treated as a daughter, a sister, a wife, or a problem — registers.

### 7.3.7 The Krakoan / mutant network

Storm, Magik, Jean Grey, and the broader Quiet Council–era network. The mutant peoplehood she once unmade has, in increments, allowed her back. This is an asset of immense psychological weight: she has experienced, at least partially, the thing her grief most denied her — *being forgiven by the wronged.*

### 7.3.8 Magneto

Asset-with-warning. Reconciled, ruptured, reconciled. Functions as a paternal node whose love is real and whose judgment is unreliable. She has, in the modern era, learned to receive his affection without obeying his strategy. This is itself a developmental milestone.

### 7.3.9 The Walk-Ins

The Orlando-era solo practice generated a wide, low-intensity network of ordinary people — witches, spirits, displaced ghosts, magical refugees — who owe her favors and remember her kindly. Diffuse, hard to map, individually small, collectively a real intelligence and logistics asset on the magical periphery.

---

## 7.4 Material and Logistical Assets

- **Residences:** the cottage / shop established in the Orlando run (door-always-open premises, currently maintained); the New Salem residual property network through Harkness; intermittent Avengers Mansion and Krakoan quarters; old Sokovian/Transian familial holdings, largely symbolic.
- **Libraries:** Harkness-inherited grimoires; the personal working library accreted over five decades; Krakoa-period access to mutant historical and biological archives; visiting privileges at the Sanctum Sanctorum.
- **Reputational capital:** within the magical community she is feared, respected, and — increasingly — consulted. Within the Avengers she is a senior figure. Within the mutant nation she is the woman who broke them and is trying to mend them; ambivalent but not exiled.
- **Information capital:** sixty years of fieldwork against most major threat actors. Personal acquaintance with Doom, Mephisto, Chthon, Loki, the Enchantress, Morgan le Fay, the Wrecking Crew, half a dozen cosmic actors. She has been inside the heads (sometimes literally) of an unusual number of opponents.

---

## 7.5 Resilience Factors — Why She Is Still Standing

This is the section that the threat-oriented files routinely omit, and it is the most important. The behavioral record contains a catastrophic decompensation in 2004–2005 and *no comparable event in the nearly twenty years since,* despite continued losses (her own death among them). The non-recurrence is not luck. It is structure.

### 7.5.1 Acquired Insight

She knows, now, what she did. She knows the mechanism — grief × capability, with no interlock. She knows the warning signs. The Orlando and Krakoa-era characterizations show a woman who *monitors herself,* who builds in friction before acting at scale, who asks before she works. Insight is not cure; it is, however, a real protective factor and she has it.

### 7.5.2 Externalized Conscience

She has deliberately constructed a network of people whose judgment she will accept *over her own* — Billy, Strange, Storm, occasionally Rogers. The decision to install external brakes is an act of mature self-knowledge. Few practitioners of her power-tier have done it.

### 7.5.3 Useful Work

The storefront, the curse-breaking, the small magics for ordinary clients. This is therapeutic in a way the clinical literature would recognize: structured, daily, prosocial activity that provides identity, contact, and small repeated experiences of being *helpful and adequate* rather than *catastrophic and culpable.* It is the closest thing to a behavioral-activation regimen she has ever had, and she designed it herself.

### 7.5.4 Survived and Integrated Death

She has died and returned. The post-resurrection presentation includes hyperactivity and guilt-drive (flagged as risk in §2), but it also includes a settledness about mortality that is rare and stabilizing. She is no longer afraid of the worst happening to *her.* This frees a great deal of cognitive bandwidth previously spent on anticipatory dread.

### 7.5.5 Forgiveness Received

From Barton, from the resurrected Vision, from Storm and elements of the mutant nation, from Billy. Each instance of being forgiven by someone with standing to refuse has been metabolized. The cumulative effect is a self-concept that, while still fragile, can now hold the proposition *people who know what I did still want me here.* This proposition is the spine of her current functioning.

### 7.5.6 Capacity for Solitude Without Collapse

A late-acquired skill, evident in the solo-era runs. She can be alone now without immediately seeking a caretaker or a team to attach to. The cottage scenes — tea, garden, cat, book, quiet — depict a woman who has built an interior life that does not require constant external regulation. Compare to the 1960s record, where solitude produced immediate distress; this is genuine development.

### 7.5.7 Tolerance for Ambiguity

She no longer requires that her own moral status be resolved. She can operate as a person who did a terrible thing *and* is doing good work, without needing to collapse the contradiction. This is a high-order ego function and it is hard-won.

### 7.5.8 Somatic Self-Care (the small ledger)

The granular record across the modern runs shows habits that read as deliberate regulation: tea ritual (consistently chamomile or rooibos in evening, black in morning); long walks; gardening (herbs, then ornamentals — the Orlando cottage); needlework and embroidery during conversation, a hands-busy stabilizer; sleep prioritized (she protects her hours, declines late operations when she can); avoidance of alcohol beyond ceremonial wine. None of this is dramatic. Cumulatively it is the daily infrastructure of someone managing a chronic condition responsibly.

### 7.5.9 The Reparative Frame Itself

The decision to organize her life around *making it right* — controversial as a clinical matter (it can collapse into self-erasure) — is, taken on its own terms, a coherent and durable meaning-structure. She knows why she gets up. The literature on prolonged grief identifies meaning-reconstruction as a core therapeutic target; she has done this work without a clinician, imperfectly, but she has done it.

### 7.5.10 The Bond Beyond Comprehension

Worth naming separately. Wiccan's existence as a reality-warper of comparable potential means she has, for the first time in her life, *a peer in the specific form of her burden.* He is also her son. The relationship is unique in the recorded universe. Whatever else it is, it is unrepeatably stabilizing.

---

## 7.6 What Makes the Assets Durable

Three structural features distinguish her asset ledger from the typical high-capability subject's:

1. **The assets are diversified across registers** — magical, relational, material, characterological, somatic. Loss of any one column leaves the others functioning. The 2004 collapse occurred precisely because nearly all columns failed simultaneously (twins gone, Vision destroyed, memory suppressed, no insight, no external brakes); the current portfolio is structured so that no single failure can reproduce that condition.
2. **The relational assets are reciprocal, not extractive.** She gives to Billy, Tommy, her clients, her teammates — and receives. Networks built on mutual exchange are more durable under stress than networks built on dependency in either direction. The Orlando-era network in particular is reciprocal almost by design.
3. **The insight is operational, not merely declarative.** She does not only *know* she is at risk; she has *built systems* to manage the risk. The externalized conscience, the small daily structure, the storefront, the deliberate non-isolation — these are interventions she has implemented, not aspirations she has stated.

---

## 7.7 Net Asset Statement

A high-capability subject with one of the most consequential power-tiers on the planet; a deep, diversified, and largely reciprocal relational network anchored by an unprecedented mother-son bond with a peer-level practitioner; a mature, operational insight into her own pathology; a self-designed daily structure that functions, in effect, as outpatient maintenance; a moral seriousness that does not flinch from her own record; a reparative project that gives her life coherent meaning; and a quiet domestic competence — tea, garden, needlework, sleep — that the file would be negligent to omit.

She has been, at her worst, the most dangerous person on Earth. She has also been, for nearly two decades and counting, *managing it.* The assets are real, they are durable, and they are — critically — *hers.* She built most of them herself, after no one else would.

— End §7. Proceed to §8 (Vulnerabilities, Liabilities & Decompensation Risk) for the obverse ledger.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION — WANDA MAXIMOFF

*UATU dossier, Section 7. The mechanics of her breaking: what conditions produce it, what the ladder looks like rung by rung, what the collapse does, and what is left standing on the other side. This is the section a containment planner reads first.*

---

## 7.1 The Governing Principle

Wanda Maximoff does not fail the way most high-capability operators fail. She does not slowly burn out, drift into substance abuse, defect to a rival faction, or harden into ideological extremism. The failure mode is **catastrophic, episodic, affect-driven, and reality-altering**, separated by long plateaus of apparent stability that are not stability at all but **over-accommodation maintained by suppression of the very content that powers the collapse**.

The governing equation, derived from the longitudinal record (Vision & Scarlet Witch #12 → West Coast Avengers #51-52 → Avengers #500-503 → House of M #1-8 → Children's Crusade → Trial of Magneto): **decompensation magnitude equals stored unmetabolized grief times instantaneous trigger salience, with capability acting as a multiplier rather than a brake**. Most subjects' breakdowns are bounded by their physical reach.
