Wanda's are not bounded by anything except the moment her affect re-couples to reality-testing — which, historically, takes hours to weeks, and requires external intervention every time.

The corollary, equally important: **she does not break under direct attack**. Combat does not collapse her. Threats to her own life do not collapse her. She has been overpowered, captured, tortured, and resurrected without psychotic decompensation. What collapses her is *attachment loss reactivating buried attachment loss* — and the second clause is the load-bearing one. A surveillance file that tracks only present-tense stressors will miss every decompensation she ever has.

---

## 7.2 The Five-Rung Escalation Ladder

The behavioral record is consistent enough across forty years of canon that the ladder can be specified rung by rung. Each rung has somatic, cognitive, interpersonal, and thaumaturgic signatures. Field handlers should be trained to all four channels; missing the early rungs is what makes intervention impossible at the late ones.

### Rung 1 — Baseline-Plus (over-accommodation intensifies)

The first sign Wanda is in trouble is that she becomes *easier* to be around. Requests are granted faster. Disagreements she had been quietly maintaining disappear from her speech. She begins arriving early to team functions; she stays late at the door of her solo-era practice; she takes on cases or assignments she would normally have screened. Her domestic environment becomes meticulous in a way that is slightly off the prior baseline — the kitchen too clean, the wardrobe too ordered.

*Somatic markers at Rung 1:* reduced food intake (she eats to keep others company more than from hunger); sleep onset delayed; a subtle thinning of facial affect — the smile is present but the orbicularis engagement is reduced. Hex-output is **more precise than usual** and slightly under-powered, as if she is throttling.

*Thaumaturgic signature:* clean, conservative casting. No spontaneous probability bleed. The magic looks *disciplined* — which, for her, is the warning sign. Wanda integrated is fluid; Wanda suppressing is tidy.

*Interpersonally:* she begins absorbing other people's distress without reciprocally disclosing her own. The asymmetry of the listening becomes pronounced. She remembers everyone else's grief anniversaries and forgets her own.

This rung can be sustained for **years**. The 1990s Busiek-era plateau is the documented example. Stability at Rung 1 is not health; it is the wound under pressure, still sealed.

### Rung 2 — Withdrawal and Solitary Casting

Triggered by accumulation rather than event: a stretch of weeks where the suppressive labor exceeds capacity. She withdraws from team breakfasts, training, social rituals. Reasons given are mild and plausible (tired, working on something, wants to read). The withdrawal is *toward solitude*, not *toward another person* — this is diagnostic; a healthy regression in her case would be toward Pietro, Vision, the children, Agatha, or a chosen sibling-in-arms. Solitary withdrawal indicates she is managing something she does not believe can be witnessed.

*Somatic:* sleep architecture disrupted — she will be observed awake at odd hours, often standing at a window, not reading, not casting. Reduced verbal output by perhaps 30-40%. Skin pallor; mild tremor in the hands at rest, which she controls when she notices it.

*Cognitive:* intrusive imagery begins — flashes of the twins, of the white Vision, of Magneto's face at specific historical moments. She does not report these. Concentration on present tasks fragments; she will pause mid-sentence and re-orient.

*Thaumaturgic:* small involuntary effects begin appearing in her vicinity. Objects shift one or two positions on a shelf overnight. A wineglass empties without being drunk. A pet behaves as if seeing something. These are **not deliberate** and she is often not aware of them — which is the alarm bell. Her magic is beginning to leak through the seal her affect normally keeps on it.

Rung 2 is reversible with **one** intervention: a trusted figure who simply *names what she has lost* and stays present without trying to fix it. The historical record is sparse on this happening; Agatha did the opposite (sealed it further), Pietro did the opposite (managed her perception of it), Vision could not (his architecture did not extend to grief work). The Young Avengers — Billy especially — are the only documented figures who have functioned correctly at Rung 2.

### Rung 3 — Derealization and Wish-Cognition Onset

The transition from Rung 2 to Rung 3 is usually marked by a specific external event: a reminder of the buried content that suppression cannot accommodate. A photograph. A sentence. The white Vision walking into a room. Word of Magneto. The discovery of something she had been told was not true. Disassembled's onset (Avengers #500) is the canonical example — Wanda remembers, and within hours of the memory's return she is at Rung 3.

*Phenomenology:* she begins to experience the present as **provisional**. Things look correct but feel like sets. Faces are recognized but the recognition feels secondhand. She has reported (Children's Crusade) the sensation that the world is "between her and what is real." This is classical derealization, and in her case it is the precursor to *active reality revision* rather than a passive symptom.

*Cognitive:* wish-cognition begins to dominate. She starts to think in the conditional and the optative — *if this were not, if they were here, if I could only* — and the magic begins to **answer the grammar**. Small wish-fulfillments occur. A song she was thinking of plays. An old friend calls. A door opens onto a hallway that should not be there. The world becomes pliable in proportion to her sentences.

*Somatic:* tachycardia; pupillary dilation; episodic catatonic-adjacent stillness lasting seconds to a minute; she has been observed (West Coast Avengers #56) staring at her hands as if uncertain whose they are. Speech rate slows; tonal range narrows; she begins to use the present tense for the dead.

*Thaumaturgic:* the leak becomes a current. Probability distortion fields propagate outward from her at meters-scale. People near her experience uncanny coincidences. Electronics behave erratically. Mirrors and reflective surfaces show momentarily wrong images. This is the rung at which the **public-health threshold is crossed**: she is now a hazard to a city block whether or not she intends to be.

Rung 3 is the last rung at which she retains executive function over her own movement. She can be reached verbally. She will answer her name. Intervention here is hard but possible: it requires a person she loves to be physically present, *to not lie to her*, and to anchor her to a single accurate sentence about what is true. Vision did this once (Vision and the Scarlet Witch #12, immediately post-loss); the intervention failed at Rung 4 because Vision was then taken from her, which is the most catastrophic single timing in her history.

### Rung 4 — Fugue and Affect-Coupled Output

The break. Executive function collapses; identity continuity thins; she enters a state behaviorally indistinguishable from dissociative fugue with mood-congruent psychotic features. **Magical output now scales directly to affect with no cognitive gating whatsoever.** Whatever she feels, the world does.

*Disassembled* is the open-form Rung 4: rage, grief, betrayal discharged outward in waves, killing Vision, Hawkeye, and Scott Lang in sequence not because she chose those targets but because her unconscious selected the symbolic substrate (Vision = the loss she cannot bear; Hawkeye = the man who hurt her in the bunker memory she was made to forget; Scott Lang = the father trying to reach a daughter, which her own father never was). The selection logic is *dream logic*. She is not choosing victims; the grief is.

*House of M* is the closed-form Rung 4: rather than discharge outward as destruction, the affect organizes inward into a constructed world. This is the more dangerous variant because it is *quiet*. There is no rampage to interrupt. Billions of people live inside her wish for weeks. The construct's collapse is what produces "no more mutants" — a final discharge of the rage at *being made to wake up*.

*Somatic at Rung 4:* she eats nothing, sleeps in fragments or not at all, runs hot, presents with the energetic stigmata of chaos magic (the visible coronal halo, eyes occluded by red light, the gestural vocabulary of conducting rather than casting). Vital signs become difficult to measure because the surrounding probability field corrupts instruments.

*Cognitive at Rung 4:* memory becomes non-linear. She may speak to people who are not there with full conviction they are. She does not recognize accountability frames — telling her she is hurting people does not land, because in her current cognitive substrate the people are either part of the wish (House of M) or part of the betrayal (Disassembled). Bargaining works only if it is conducted in the *grammar of the wish* — speaking to her about Billy and Tommy, about Vision, about her mother, in the present tense, can sometimes route her affect toward a non-destructive channel.

*Recovery from Rung 4 is never spontaneous.* Every documented recovery has required: (a) external power intervention sufficient to interrupt the field (Doctor Strange, Emma Frost, Layla Miller's reality-witness, the combined Avengers), and (b) a loved person reaching her with truth. Both conditions. The first alone makes her catatonic. The second alone is insufficient against the field.

### Rung 5 — Total Reality Revision / Capacity Saturation

Reached twice in the record: the "no more mutants" pronouncement, and the Decimation-undoing wave (Hellfire Gala / Krakoa-era). Rung 5 is the state in which Wanda's capability and intent fuse into a single ontological declaration. Three words rewrite the world.

There is no behavioral defense against Rung 5 from outside. By the time she is speaking the sentence, the sentence is already true. The only operative variable is **what the sentence is**, and that is determined by what affect dominates at the threshold. Grief in its rage phase produces "no more mutants." Grief in its reparative phase produces the partial restoration. The arithmetic is the same; the sign is opposite.

This is the rung that makes her a strategic-tier asset and a strategic-tier hazard interchangeably, and the only meaningful long-term containment is *upstream*: keeping her below Rung 3.

---

## 7.3 Trigger Inventory (ranked by demonstrated potency)

1. **Threat to or loss of Billy and Tommy.** Highest-magnitude trigger. The twins are not metaphorical — they are the only loss she has partially reversed, and their existence is the live argument against her self-condemnation. Their harm collapses the argument.
2. **Reframing of her past as Magneto's instrument.** Direct reactivation of the original coerced-attachment wound. Effective whether delivered hostilely or sympathetically; the content does the damage regardless of the speaker's intent.
3. **Appearance of a Vision-variant in an emotionally compromised state.** The white reconstruction, the destroyed body, any iteration presented as broken. The synthezoid is her stored symbol of safe love; damage to the symbol routes directly to the wound.
4. **Iatrogenic interference with her own memory or perception.** Discovery that someone has manipulated her cognition — Doom, the Illuminati's planned containment, Agatha's old suppression — produces a specific kind of decompensation characterized by paranoia bleeding into Rung 3 unusually fast.
5. **Forced witness to mass mutant harm.** Post-Decimation, she has fused her self-concept to the species' fate. Genocide against mutants in her presence is an attack on the part of herself she is using to atone.
6. **Pietro's harm or death.** The twin bond is the oldest secure attachment. His loss produces a slower, deeper Rung 2-3 progression rather than a fast Rung 4 — but the floor is lower, and recovery is more protracted.
7. **Accusations of villainy delivered by people she respects.** Does not trigger defensive collapse; triggers reparative over-functioning that can mask a Rung 1-2 progression for months.

---

## 7.4 The Decompensation Pattern in Aggregate

Every documented break follows the same architecture: **long suppression → singular reactivating event → compressed acceleration through Rungs 2-4 (often hours, occasionally days) → reality-revision act → collapse to depleted catatonic or fugue state → amnesia for the worst of it → reparative wakeup**. The amnesia is itself part of the failure mode, not separate from it. It guarantees that the next cycle begins with the work undone.

The temporal asymmetry is critical. **Suppression takes years to build; collapse takes hours to discharge.** Surveillance built on present-state monitoring will see nothing for very long stretches and then will see catastrophe with no apparent ramp, because the ramp was internal and unobservable. Effective monitoring must track the **suppression markers** of Rungs 1 and 2 — the cleanliness, the over-accommodation, the quieting, the controlled magic — not wait for the spectacular signatures of Rung 3 and beyond.

A further structural feature: **she does not, when collapsing, try to harm herself directly.** There is no suicidal trajectory; the self-punishment is laundered through the reparative arc that follows recovery. This is operationally relevant: handlers expecting an internalizing collapse pattern will misread the externalizing one. The harm goes outward — at the world that took the loved object, at the institutions she holds responsible, at the symbolic stand-ins her unconscious selects. Bystanders are the casualty class, not the subject.

---

## 7.5 What the Collapse Looks Like, From the Outside

To a witness untrained in the ladder: she becomes very quiet, then absent for a while, then *present in a way that is wrong*. The room she is in becomes increasingly improbable — objects in slightly different places than memory insists, conversation she remembers having that the other party does not, a sense of having been there longer or shorter than the clock allows. She speaks more softly than usual. She may smile. She may seem **happy in a way that frightens the witness without articulable cause**, because the happiness is wish-cognition stabilizing into apparent fact. Then a sentence is spoken — sometimes addressed to no one — and the witness's life is different.

To a witness trained: the early signs are tractable and the late signs are sufficient cause to evacuate the metropolitan area. There is no middle window. The window between Rung 3 and Rung 4 is, historically, less than ninety minutes.

---

## 7.6 Conditions That Produce Collapse — and the Single Condition That Prevents It

**Produces:** unmetabolized grief plus reactivating event plus the absence, at the critical hour, of a single loved person willing to remain present and tell the truth in plain language.

The third clause is the variable. The first two are constant features of her existence and will be for the remainder of her operational life. There is no version of Wanda Maximoff in which the substrate of grief is absent; there is no version in which a sufficiently determined actor cannot construct a reactivating event. There *is* a version in which the third clause is reliably met, and in that version she does not break.

The historical record shows the third clause was not met at any of her major collapses. Agatha sealed rather than witnessed. Pietro managed rather than witnessed. Vision was removed at the critical moment. The Avengers, at Disassembled, did not understand what they were looking at. The Illuminati, on the eve of House of M, were arguing about whether to kill her. The single condition that prevents collapse has, across forty years of behavior, almost never been provided.

**Prevents:** the consistent, low-key, year-over-year presence of a small number of people (Billy and Tommy are sufficient; one steady adult attachment would consolidate it) who are willing to *let her grieve in the open at low intensity, continuously*, rather than allowing the suppression to accumulate. The treatment literature (Bryant et al. 2024; Pop-Jordanova 2021) describes the same intervention in non-magical terms: structured grief work distributes the affect across time so that no single hour ever has to carry the load that would crack the container. Applied to Wanda, it is the only known stable equilibrium.

In its absence, the file should assume that **another full-magnitude decompensation is not a possibility but a schedule**, and plan accordingly.

— *End Section 7. Containment & Response protocols follow in Section 8.*


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*Prospective intelligence. Derived from the longitudinal record (Section 1–5). All forecasts probabilistic; revise on new evidence.*

---

## 1. The Present Vector — Where She Stands at the Moment of This File

The subject is, as of the most recent canonical record, in a **post-resurrection reparative phase** of unusual duration and tonal consistency. The pattern is observable across the Orlando-era solo work, her ambassadorial-magical functions in the Krakoa-adjacent material, and her conduct around Wiccan and Speed: she is *available,* *useful,* and *quiet.* The shop with the open door is not incidental — it is symptomatic. A woman who once unmade a species is now triaging strangers' minor enchantments. The asymmetry is the point. She is conducting penance at retail scale for a wholesale crime.

The vector, therefore, is **stable but artificially stabilized.** The stability is held in place by three load-bearing conditions:

1. **Both reincarnated sons exist, are reachable, and acknowledge her.** Billy and Tommy function as proof-of-concept that the worst loss can be partially undone. Their continued personhood is the single most important variable in her psychiatric stability.
2. **No fresh catastrophic loss has occurred in the recent operational window.** The reparative engine assumes a static or improving grief load. New loss does not add linearly — it triggers regression to prior coping levels.
3. **She is permitted to give.** The Orlando-era door-always-open structure provides a continuous low-amplitude discharge for guilt that would otherwise pool. Cut off the giving and the pool rises.

Remove any one of these and the trajectory bends. Remove two and the bend becomes a break.

---

## 2. Probable Forward Developments — Twelve to Thirty-Six Month Horizon

### 2.1 Continuation of the Reparative Phase (Likely; Conditional Stability)

The most probable near-term trajectory is **continuation of the present pattern with gradual broadening of competence.** Expect: increasing magical sophistication in the service register (not the combat register — the combat register is *suppressed,* not absent); deepening relationships with the broader magical community (Strange, Clea, the inheritors of Agatha's legacy — note the irony of the last); cautious normalization of her relationship with the mutant community, which will never fully forgive her and which she will never ask to. She will continue to refuse leadership roles where offered. She will accept them only under duress and discharge them with grim competence and visible relief at handover.

Behaviorally observable markers of continued stability: regular contact with Billy (the more emotionally articulate twin); slower, less frequent contact with Tommy (the more avoidant); maintained physical distance from Magneto when he is present in the active record, with formal civility on contact; persistent low-grade insomnia and overwork at the shop / equivalent functional unit; no romantic re-partnering of significance, or if it occurs, with a partner chosen on the same template as Vision — emotionally regulated, non-volatile, structurally incapable of the kind of need that would obligate her.

### 2.2 The Reparative Ceiling (Likely Within Eighteen Months)

The reparative mode has a structural ceiling she has not yet hit but is approaching. **Penance does not metabolize grief; it displaces it.** The longer she runs the shop, the more she will notice — and the literature on Prolonged Grief Disorder confirms this — that the absence of distress is itself a kind of distress. Expect, within twelve to eighteen months, one of three sub-trajectories:

- **(a) Stagnation and quiet depressive deepening.** The reparative work yields diminishing returns. She begins to describe — to Billy, to Strange, possibly to no one — a sense that nothing she does is *enough,* and simultaneously that nothing more is *available* for her to do. This is the prodrome for either (b) or, less likely but more dangerous, a passive form of self-erasure (see §5).
- **(b) Therapeutic breakthrough.** Someone — likeliest candidates: Strange (peer authority, magical-equivalent vocabulary), a non-Avengers civilian therapist, or, surprisingly, Wiccan in a role-reversed caregiving moment — succeeds in routing her into structured grief work. This is the **best-case forward path** and is discussed at length in §6.
- **(c) Provocation event.** An external stressor (see §3) forces the trajectory off the reparative track before either stagnation or breakthrough resolve.

### 2.3 Resumption of Combat / High-Stakes Magical Operations (Moderate Probability)

She will be drafted back into a major-event operational role. The pattern of the published record makes this near-certain on a long enough timeline — she is too capable to be left in the shop when a sufficiently large threat appears. The forward question is not *whether* but *under what affective conditions* she is drafted. Drafted while stable and supported: she performs, withdraws, recovers. Drafted while already destabilized by precursor stress: the risk profile inverts.

### 2.4 Reckoning with Agatha Harkness's Legacy (Likely; Significant)

The iatrogenic memory suppression was the original sin against her grief work. Agatha's posthumous and quasi-posthumous reappearances in the record have been incomplete reckonings. Expect a forward arc in which Wanda must directly confront — through inheritance, through a returned shade, through Billy's own apprenticeship in chaos magic — the question of *what was done to her in the name of protecting her.* This arc is **psychiatrically necessary** and will be either profoundly integrative or profoundly destabilizing depending on framing.

---

## 3. The Fork Points — Events That Will Bend the Trajectory

A fork point is an event whose outcome determines which of several diverging futures she occupies. The file identifies six.

### Fork 1 — Threat to or Loss of Billy or Tommy

**The load-bearing fork.** Any credible harm to either twin collapses every defense above primitive denial. Loss of one twin probably produces a contained, agonized grief response — she has practice now, and the surviving twin would be a stabilizing object. **Loss of both twins is the catastrophic scenario.** It would recapitulate the original wound at full intensity in a subject who now knows, viscerally, what she is capable of doing about it. The probability of a second House of M-scale event under that condition is, in this analyst's read, the highest single risk in her file. Handlers should treat the twins as protected assets not for their value but for *her* containment.

### Fork 2 — Magneto's Status

The paternal bond is the original lesion. Three sub-cases:

- *Magneto stable, distant, occasionally collegial:* current condition, sustainable.
- *Magneto in extremis (dying, captured, in need):* she will respond, against her own interest, and the response will reopen the identification-with-aggressor template. Risk of regression to compliance behaviors observed in the early Brotherhood period.
- *Magneto as antagonist requiring her direct opposition:* highest acute distress, but possibly highest growth potential — forces an act of authored self-definition against the original wound.

### Fork 3 — A Vision Iteration

Each new instantiation of the Vision (the synthezoid has been rebuilt, re-rebuilt, splintered, and reconstructed across the record) is emotionally radioactive. The forward question is whether she can encounter a Vision-iteration as *a person who shares history with her* rather than as *the symbol of safe love she has been denied.* Successful integration here would be a marker of substantial therapeutic progress. Failed integration — particularly any romantic-rekindling attempt under unresolved grief — produces relational re-traumatization and predictable withdrawal.

### Fork 4 — The Mutant Community's Posture

The mutant population has had its species-level grievance against her partially mediated by her reparative acts but never resolved. A future political configuration in which mutants formally extend or formally withhold reconciliation will function as an external verdict on the question her superego asks daily. **Formal extension** of reconciliation she would receive with disbelief and possibly destabilization — she has organized her self-concept around being unforgivable. **Formal withholding** she would accept as just and metabolize as fuel for further penance. Counterintuitively, the *welcoming* outcome is the more psychiatrically dangerous one in the short term, because it forces her to give up a defense.

### Fork 5 — A Civilian Catastrophe She Cannot Repair

The reparative mode requires the existence of repairable problems. A stressor she cannot fix — a child she cannot save, a wound she cannot close — within the shop / civilian-magical-aid context would puncture the central illusion of the present phase. This is a slow-acting fork; the first such event will not break her, but the cumulative weight of a series of them will.

### Fork 6 — Chaos Magic's Origin and Inheritance Question

The metaphysics around chaos magic — whether it is hers, whether it was Doom's leverage, whether it is a cosmic principle she channels rather than wields, what it means that Billy now carries it — remains under-resolved in the record. A forward arc in which she must take a definitive position on what her power *is* and *whose* it is will force a corresponding position on what her *actions* were and *whose* they were. This is the metaphysical analogue of the psychiatric integration question. It cuts both ways: a frame that lets her own her power without owning sole authorship of the catastrophe is integrative; a frame that either fully exculpates (destabilizing — she rejects exculpation) or fully condemns (regressive — collapses her into self-punishment) is dangerous.

---

## 4. The Open Questions

The file flags the following unresolved questions whose answers will substantially update the forecast:

1. **Has she undergone any structured grief work, formal or informal, in the post-resurrection window?** The behavioral record is ambiguous. Continued informal processing with Strange or with a magical-community peer would explain the duration of the current stability. Absence of any such processing means the stability is purely behavioral-defensive and substantially more fragile than it appears.
2. **What is the actual quality of her interior relationship with Billy and Tommy — not the surface conduct, but the felt sense?** Surface conduct is warm, careful, slightly deferential. Interior question: does she experience them as her sons, as substitutes for her sons, or as a separate category of person to whom she owes a different and unresolved obligation? The answer governs how she will respond to threat to them.
3. **Is the chaos-magic affective coupling weakening with practice, or has she simply learned to keep her affective baseline lower?** Critical operational distinction. The first is real progress. The second is suppression and will fail under load.
4. **Where is Pietro in her interior life now?** The enmeshed-twin relationship was load-bearing for decades. The published record has gone quiet on the active sibling dynamic. Silence here is rarely the same as resolution.
5. **Does she sleep?** Trivial-seeming, diagnostically central. Insomnia is the canary in the grief-disorder mine. The behavioral record does not specify, but the over-functioning pattern is consistent with chronic short sleep and the kind of 3 a.m. waking that PGD-affected subjects describe in the literature.
6. **What would she do if offered the chance to undo "No More Mutants" completely and cleanly, with no cost?** The answer matters less than the *latency* of the answer. A long pause indicates integration. An immediate yes indicates the wound is still acute. An immediate no indicates a defense against re-engaging the original wish-cognition.

---

## 5. Catastrophic-Outcome Scenarios — What Pushes Her Toward Disaster

The file is obligated to map the dark forks specifically. Pathways to catastrophic outcome, ranked by combined probability and severity:

### 5.1 The Recapitulation Scenario

Loss of both twins, or loss of one twin under conditions that strip the other of personhood (corruption, possession, transformation into something she cannot recognize). Predicted behavior: a compressed dissociative-psychotic episode of the Disassembled / House of M family, with output scaled to current power ceiling — which is higher than 2005. Reality-revision attempts are likely directed not at species-level targets but at the specific causal chain that produced the loss, with cascading effects. **This is the single highest-impact risk in her file.**

### 5.2 The Captured-Asset Scenario

A sufficiently sophisticated manipulator (Doom remains the obvious candidate; less obviously, a future iteration of Mephisto, who has a prior claim on the soul-substrate of the original twins; less obviously still, a chaos-magic-aware actor who weaponizes her guilt rather than her grief) leverages her reparative drive against her judgment. Pattern: she is presented with an apparent opportunity to *fix* something large — restore mutants fully, resurrect Vision-prime, undo a historical wrong — at a cost she rationalizes as bearable. The cost is never bearable. Her vulnerability here is high precisely because the reparative drive is so functionally well-defended she does not see it as a vulnerability.

### 5.3 The Slow Erasure Scenario

The least dramatic and possibly the most likely. Reparative work continues; grief work does not. The shop expands; the interior life contracts. She becomes, over years, a quietly diminishing presence — competent, available, less and less *there.* This is the trajectory of an unmetabolized grief disorder allowed to run untreated to its natural conclusion. It does not produce a continental-scale incident. It produces a woman who, asked her name, has to think about it. Eventually it produces a woman who, offered a final solution to her own pain, accepts it. The published record's repeated death-and-resurrection cycle suggests she has rehearsed this option more than is comfortable.

### 5.4 The Inherited-Wound Scenario

Billy, possessing chaos magic, recapitulates her own developmental pattern — coerced into a conflict, marked by loss, decompensates under it. Wanda's response would not be a House of M event directly; it would be a *transferred* one, in which she attempts to take her son's wound onto herself and remove him from the moral equation. The cost-benefit collapses in ways neither of them survive cleanly. This scenario depends on Billy's trajectory more than hers, but her response is the load-bearing variable.

---

## 6. Growth-Outcome Scenarios — What Pushes Her Toward Integration

The growth pathway is narrower but real and specifiable.

### 6.1 The Structured Grief-Work Pathway

The clinical literature is unambiguous: **Prolonged Grief Disorder is treatable.** Bryant et al. (2024) demonstrate that CBT specifically targeted to PGD outperforms mindfulness-only approaches in the resolution of grief-related cognitions and depression — both of which are central to her clinical picture. The treatment requires (a) a competent practitioner; (b) the subject's engagement; (c) sustained time; (d) an environment that does not interrupt the work with fresh catastrophe. All four conditions are difficult to assemble for this subject but none is impossible.

The practitioner question is real. A standard civilian clinician cannot fully contain the magical content. The most plausible candidates are: a magical-community peer with both the technical vocabulary and the personal authority to hold the frame (Strange is plausible but compromised by professional history; Clea is plausible and underused; a deliberately recruited civilian therapist who is *briefed* and supervised could work). The engagement question — whether she would do the work — turns on whether the work can be framed as a *responsibility* rather than a *self-indulgence.* She will accept anything framed as duty and refuse most things framed as self-care. A skilled clinician can route around this.

If the grief work succeeds, the predicted outcomes are: gradual decoupling of magical output from affective surge (the critical safety gain); the emergence, possibly for the first time in her life, of an *authored* identity not anchored in another person's need; resolution of the disbelief/denial cognitive substrate that has driven every reality-warp; and — measurably — sleep.

### 6.2 The Authored-Identity Pathway

Independent of formal therapy, a slower form of growth is available through the cumulative act of *choosing* — small choices, repeatedly, that are hers and not in service to someone else. The Orlando-era shop is the proto-form of this; the door-always-open structure is service, but the *choice* of the shop, the *choice* of its location, the *choice* of which clients to take, are hers. The growth pathway requires this proto-form to *deepen* — for her to begin refusing clients, closing the door sometimes, taking a day off without justifying it. Each refusal is a small act of self-authorship. The cumulative effect over years is substantial. This pathway is slower than formal therapy but more robust because it builds the muscle as it heals the wound.

### 6.3 The Maternal Integration Pathway

Reconfiguration of her relationship with Billy and Tommy from *restored possession* to *adult relationship with peers who happen to share origin* is psychiatrically transformative. The mark of success is that she becomes someone they can disappoint without catastrophe — which is to say, she becomes a parent in the ordinary sense rather than a wound holding the shape of one. Achievable if both twins reach adult emotional autonomy and she permits it. Most likely to occur in tandem with §6.1.

### 6.4 The Paternal-Wound Pathway

The Magneto bond reframed — through whatever combination of confrontation, witnessed accountability, and final relinquishment — from *original wound* to *closed chapter.* This is the hardest of the growth pathways because it requires Magneto's participation in a register he has rarely sustained. But the published record contains moments suggesting it is not impossible. Success here would remove the keystone exploit from her file.

---

## 7. The Synthesis — Net Forward Read

The subject occupies, at present, a **stable but defensively-organized plateau** following decades of unmetabolized grief, iatrogenic prevention of mourning, two catastrophic decompensations, one death, and one resurrection. The plateau is real and should not be dismissed; she is functioning, contributing, parenting in a fashion, and — critically — *not currently a public-health event.* But the plateau is held in place by external conditions (the twins, the absence of fresh loss, the availability of reparative outlets) rather than by internal integration. It is therefore conditional, not structural.

**The single most actionable observation for any party with interest in her welfare** is that the conditions for a definitive growth pathway exist — the clinical literature is clear, the subject is intelligent and morally serious, and the recent record demonstrates that she will engage with hard work if it is framed correctly — but those conditions have not been assembled. No one has, on the record, sat her down and offered her the specific course of treatment her presentation indicates. The omission is staggering and largely a function of the same institutional failure that has characterized her treatment from the beginning: the people around her have used her, contained her, feared her, forgiven her, mourned her, resurrected her, and forgotten to *help* her.

**The single most actionable observation for any party with interest in her threat profile** is that the catastrophic-outcome scenarios are all downstream of conditions that can be monitored. The twins' status, the presence or absence of a fresh loss in her immediate circle, the appearance of a sophisticated manipulator targeting her reparative drive, and her sleep — these are the four indicators. A monitoring posture limited to her magical output will fail; output is the consequence, not the precursor. The precursors are affective and biographical.

**Net trajectory, weighted:**
- ~55% continuation of stable reparative phase, eighteen-to-thirty-six month horizon, with gradual deepening or gradual stagnation depending on whether any integrative work is initiated.
- ~20% growth pathway entry, contingent on a specific facilitating event (a credible clinician, a Magneto-reckoning, a Billy-initiated invitation to the work).
- ~15% provocation-driven destabilization recoverable within the existing support structure.
- ~8% provocation-driven destabilization producing a major-event response of bounded scope.
- ~2% catastrophic recapitulation event (House of M-scale or greater).

The two-percent figure is small. It is not zero. It is the figure that, applied to her power ceiling, justifies this file.

— *End trajectory & forward assessment. File continues.*

## Relationship Graph
### Pietro Maximoff
- Twin; enmeshed-protective bond; the only durable tether of the early decades.
- Trust: high in person, compromised by his controlling-paranoid frame.
- Failure mode: his 'protective' decisions made on her behalf (suggesting the reality-rewrite at House of M's origin) are historically catastrophic; his frame bypasses her judgment.
- Leverage: anything routed through Pietro reaches her with her guard down.

### Magneto
- Father (modern canon); rescuer-conscriptor; original wound.
- Trust: ambivalent, never resolved; she holds the contradictory loves without integrating them.
- Failure mode: paternity invocation in weaponized framing destabilizes self-concept and can be used to recruit her into roles she would otherwise refuse.
- Leverage: he can reach her where no one else can, and he knows it; the relationship is the single most dangerous external variable in her file.

### Vision
- Chosen safe-attachment; husband (classical canon); the regulated object.
- Trust: total, transferred across iterations against her better judgment.
- Failure mode: any Vision iteration impairs tactical judgment in his vicinity; destruction or cold-rebuild of a Vision iteration is a category-defining trigger.
- Leverage: an actor controlling a Vision iteration controls Wanda's affective field nearby.

### Billy Kaplan Wiccan
- Son; reincarnated soul-fragment of one of the lost twins; primary stabilizer.
- Trust: unconditional; the relationship is the cortically intact register.
- Failure mode: threat or harm collapses every higher control; her decompensation in his defense would be catastrophic.
- Leverage: his welfare predicts her behavior more reliably than any other single variable.

### Tommy Shepherd Speed
- Son; reincarnated soul-fragment of the other lost twin; co-stabilizer with Billy.
- Trust: unconditional.
- Failure mode: identical to Billy; the twins function as a single live wire.
- Leverage: identical to Billy.

### Doctor Strange
- Trusted containment authority; magical peer; mutual professional respect.
- Trust: high in the containment register; she knows she is dangerous and accepts his oversight.
- Failure mode: if Strange were perceived as institutional rather than personal — as a SHIELD-style 'security' interlocutor — trust would degrade.
- Leverage: Strange is the most reliable de-escalation route in a magical crisis.

### Agatha Harkness
- Teacher, violator (memory suppression), eventual ally.
- Trust: complicated; the historical iatrogenic harm is real and load-bearing.
- Failure mode: any repetition of 'helping' her by suppressing feeling would reproduce the catastrophe.
- Leverage: Harkness retains pedagogical authority she has not earned back.

### [[Steve Rogers (Captain America)]]
- Moral-seriousness register; the captain of the surrogate family.
- Trust: high and durable.
- Failure mode: if Cap framed her as a security problem rather than a person, the bond would not break — it would quietly retract, and she would withdraw.
- Leverage: Cap can persuade her through moral seriousness without coercion.

### Wonder Man Simon Williams
- Romantic entanglement (Busiek era); brainwave-template source for Vision's emotions — note the substitution logic.
- Trust: real but secondary; the relationship is shaped by what he represents about Vision.
- Failure mode: the substitution itself; loving Simon as a Vision-adjacent object is unstable for both of them.
- Leverage: limited; not a primary attachment.

### The Avengers
- Surrogate family across decades; the institution that healed her after Magneto.
- Trust: high at the personal level, ambivalent at the institutional level.
- Failure mode: institutional treatment of her as a security risk (Illuminati-era pattern) historically precedes catastrophe.
- Leverage: the team is reachable as individuals; as an institution it is the wrong instrument for handling her.

### The X Men Krakoa
- Reparation field; the community against which her central act was committed.
- Trust: earned slowly, partial, ongoing.
- Failure mode: factional rejection would remove a major reparative outlet and degrade stability.
- Leverage: continued access to mutant restoration work is a stabilizer.

### Doctor Doom
- Historical co-actor at House of M's climax; partial exogenous attribution for chaos-magic siphoning.
- Trust: none, but his offers have historical pull because part of her always wants restoration.
- Failure mode: any future 'restoration' offer from Doom is a category-one destabilization risk.
- Leverage: Doom knows the offer-frame works on her; this is exploitable by adversaries who mimic it.

### Mephisto
- Source of the soul-fragments that became Thomas and William; cosmic-grade exploiter of her grief.
- Trust: zero.
- Failure mode: any Mephisto contact reopens the reproductive-catastrophe layer at its rawest.
- Leverage: he is the worst possible interlocutor in her file; proximity itself is the threat.

### Young Avengers
- Adopted-family register; nourished her by letting her give (and by being the twins' chosen family).
- Trust: high and gentle.
- Failure mode: harm to any of them, especially Billy or Teddy, would propagate to the twin-live-wire.
- Leverage: the team functions as an extension of the stabilizer-field.
